Details of the Meeting of the Nineteen-Member Committee the Day Before Yesterday 11

(Geneva) Today (14th), the meeting of the Nineteen-Member Committee was characterized by complete unanimity. It began with a discussion of the letter from Japan, followed by the drafting of a response. The assembly then discussed the Jehol problem and decided to notify the Japanese representative that any aggravation of the situation would undermine new efforts at mediation. The assembly then passed a proposal with minor, insignificant amendments and supplemented the section on the selection of members for the negotiating committee, deciding that the negotiating committee should be composed of the following representatives:

(1) Members of the Nineteen-Member Committee who volunteer to join. This point was clarified because the negotiations may take place in the Far East, and anyone wishing to participate must be prepared to travel to the Far East to work.

(2) Signatory countries of the Nine-Power Treaty and Soviet Russia.

Decision to End Mediation at the General Assembly 12

The assembly also decided that the meeting of the League of Nations General Assembly on Tuesday should discuss and decide on the conclusion of the mediation. A second meeting will be held three days later to discuss this report. It is expected that the League of Nations General Assembly will also hold a third and final meeting on Saturday.

Proposal's Shortcoming: No Deadline Specified 13

During today's meeting, Irish representative Lester asked what would happen if one of the parties rejected the proposal. Secretary-General Drummond replied that he believed there should be a three-month grace period, after which a new report would be submitted to the League of Nations General Assembly. However, the point raised by Ireland was unclear, which is why the proposal did not mention a grace period.

Belgian representative Boelcon said that he had spoken with Chinese representative Dr. Yen Hui-ching before the meeting, and Dr. Yen believed that the proposal still had a shortcoming, namely, that it did not specify a deadline. Dr. Yen asked people to pay attention to the need for a deadline.

How to Deal with Japan Ignoring Advice 14

The assembly believed that the proposal had not yet been submitted to both parties, so their opinions could not be considered immediately. However, it was felt that Irish representative Lester had pointed out a weakness, as the League of Nations Covenant was ambiguous on this point. There is a serious gap here. If Japan ignores the proposal, how will it be dealt with? Article 12 of the League of Nations Covenant only states that member states may not engage in war until three months after the League of Nations General Assembly has submitted a report. Although the majority of the Nineteen-Member Committee believed that the League of Nations could not wash its hands of the matter, no one could say what steps should be taken under the Covenant.

Invitations to Organize Negotiation Meeting Issued 15

The assembly believed that if negotiations do not materialize, the committee appointed by the League of Nations to monitor the negotiations between the two sides will also serve as an agency to observe the development of the situation. It is reported that invitations will be sent to all members of the Nineteen-Member Committee and the three countries of the Netherlands, the United States, and Russia tonight, so that their replies can be obtained as soon as possible, and the negotiating committee can be organized next Tuesday. The assembly believes that not all members of the Nineteen-Member Committee will accept the invitation, as it is expected that the negotiating location will be in the Far East. Although the door to mediation has not been closed before Tuesday, the assembly believes that Japan will not change its attitude.

Matsuoka Will Make a Big Speech at the General Assembly 16

Today, the Japanese spokesperson hinted that Matsuoka will make an important gesture when the League of Nations General Assembly holds an open meeting, announcing Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations. However, the general public believes that Japan will not take this drastic action immediately. Japan may wait and see how things develop before deciding on concrete actions. However, when the League of Nations General Assembly meets on Tuesday, the Chinese and Japanese representatives will inevitably make important speeches. At the last meeting of the League of Nations General Assembly, Matsuoka made a big speech because he did not recognize the "Manchukuo" issue. The proposal now explicitly stipulates that "Manchukuo" will not be recognized, which may cause Matsuoka to make another big speech.

Meeting Place Communiqué The League of Nations issued a communiqué tonight, the full text of which is as follows:

The Nineteen-Member Committee met this afternoon and first considered the reply from Japanese Chief Delegate Matsuoka to the Committee regarding the questions asked on February 9. It was agreed that the Secretary-General should reply on behalf of the Committee. The Committee then read and reviewed the first draft of the revised text submitted yesterday and subsequently passed the first three paragraphs of the report. If mediation fails, this report will be submitted to the League of Nations General Assembly in accordance with Section 4 of Article 15 of the Covenant. The Committee then proceeded to the fourth paragraph of the report, namely the first reading of the proposal, which was slightly modified and passed. The General Assembly decided to convene on Tuesday next week. The full text of the League of Nations General Assembly report will be distributed to all members of the League of Nations as soon as it is printed, probably at the end of this week. At the same time, it will be broadcast by the League of Nations radio station via wireless and wire, reaching the government radio stations or telecommunications bureaus of various countries (Reuters dispatch, 14th).

Japanese Residents in London Host Lord Lytton at a Banquet 17

(London) The Japanese Students' Association of the University of London hosted Lord Lytton at a Japanese restaurant in London last night. Many Japanese residents attended the banquet. Lord Lytton delivered a speech at the banquet, stating that he did not believe in resorting to war to enforce peace. The League of Nations can only do one thing, namely, clearly and practically define the scope within which the Sino-Japanese dispute should be resolved, and that it should be in accordance with the obligations of the League of Nations Covenant. To say that the League of Nations can adopt a system of war or reconciliation, or use a "big stick" to force a member state to accept its views, is simply empty talk. Lytton also stated that a solution to the Sino-Japanese dispute can be found within the rules and regulations of the League of Nations Covenant (Reuters dispatch, 15th).

British Economic Circles Are Only Thinking of Themselves 18

Avoiding the Use of Article 16

(London) Responsible persons in British economic circles are extremely concerned about the situation in the Far East. What attitude should Britain take once China and Japan formally declare war? This is a matter of great concern to the general public. The hostile actions of China and Japan are in serious violation of the League of Nations Covenant signed by Britain. The British government cannot stand idly by, but it seems that Britain is unwilling to take retaliatory measures against the aggressor or adopt sanctions. What can be believed is that Britain will do its utmost within the scope of the League of Nations. As for implementing sanctions in accordance with Article 16 of the Covenant, this involves a great deal, and the countries concerned must be prepared to cope with any eventuality before it can be realized. It is feared that this level is difficult to achieve. People here believe that even if Japan's crimes are clearly declared in accordance with the provisions of Article 15, it will be enough to make Japan withdraw from the League of Nations, and there is no need to apply the sanctions of Article 16. If Japan withdraws from the League of Nations, Britain can take two paths: either prevent Japan from withdrawing, so as not to reduce the authority of the League of Nations, or allow it to withdraw, and let the League of Nations reduce its scope, because the scope is too large, and the interests are too complicated, and any effective joint action cannot be carried out, and it is better to reduce the scope. As of now, the first method has been regarded as a creed by all except the Liberal Party and the opposition. Although some formal personnel have expressed their support for the second method, the prospect of success is still far away, because the slogan adopted by Britain in international policy in recent years is "striving for mediation" (Havas dispatch, 14th).

Geneva Newspapers' Views on the League of Nations 19

(Geneva) The work of the Sino-Japanese dispute in Geneva will now be silent until next Tuesday. The comments made by various Geneva newspapers on the resolution of the Nineteen-Member Committee are extremely different. One side views the resolution to continue negotiations, that is, the disguised "mediation procedure, as evidence of the League of Nations' weakness. The newspapers holding this view said that the League of Nations' universalism now clearly contains dangerous microorganisms, which will endanger the noble ideals that the League of Nations possessed at the time of its establishment. The United States has not joined the League of Nations, and the Soviet system has broken away from the League of Nations and is active, which has limited the League of Nations' power and authority. Now it is urgent to consolidate the Covenant and make a clear and practical interpretation, otherwise it cannot be hoped that the League of Nations will intervene in the dispute and achieve results, regardless of whether the dispute occurs in the Far East or South America. Other newspapers hold the opposite view, saying that the resolution of the League of Nations is a victory for the League of Nations' principles and a great success for small countries. In the first few acts of the dispute, the great powers were extremely unwilling to take any clear stance. Through the struggle of the small countries, they finally dragged them into the same front. The newspaper also believes that when the time is right, more severe actions can be taken, and small countries can still use their power to influence powerful neighbors and achieve victory (Reuters dispatch, 15th).

Cecil Launches Peace Shop 20

Opposing the Use of Force to Resolve International Disputes

Japanese Brutality is the Enemy of World Civilization

(London) Former British representative to the League of Nations, Lord Cecil, opened a "Peace Shop" in the Chelsea district of London to promote peace and improve the lives of the unemployed. It officially opened today. Cecil claimed that his purpose was to make the British people feel interested in international events, "and said that the universe is shrinking day by day, and all countries are mutually involved in an inseparable relationship, and the conflict between China and Japan in the Far East is in full swing, but our people are indifferent to it. What we should know about the Far East is not who Manchuria belongs to, but the real question is whether international disputes should be resolved by violence. A strong country in the Far East is now trying to force a weaker nation to submit to its will by force. If this kind of brutality is recognized by the world, it is tantamount to the recurrence of the situation of the European War in 1914 today, and the blood and sweat that mankind has used to seek peace after the European War will all be in vain" (Havas dispatch, 14th).

Current Affairs Commentary

The Serious Period Has Arrived... National Reflection Yuan 21

The League of Nations has recently suddenly changed its hesitant attitude and resolutely upheld justice. The Nineteen-Member Committee has passed the entire draft report, which can be said to be a major failure for Japanese diplomacy. However, we should not be complacent and relax our spirit of struggle, thinking that diplomacy is helping us, or take advantage of the opportunity of the League of Nations' break with Japan to think that we can hide in a corner and sit back and reap the benefits, or think that Japan will succumb to the pressure of the League of Nations and eventually yield and obey. If we think that our country can be slightly relieved from now on, then we are greatly mistaken.

Although the League of Nations has passed the report in the Nineteen-Member Committee today, it is still unknown whether there will be changes in the General Assembly in the future. Even if there are no changes, it can pass smoothly like the Nineteen-Member Committee. However, after the passage, if the League of Nations does not take further steps to pressure Japan with the sanctions of Article 16 of the Covenant, then the effect of the report is also equal to zero. At present, the atmosphere in the League of Nations seems to be very激昂, but it is still trying to avoid the use of Article 16. Because it is closely related to its own interests and there are many disputes, it has no courage to implement it resolutely. According to yesterday's foreign telegram, the leaders of the League of Nations expect that the pressure applied to Japan will be based on the Nine-Power Treaty and the Kellogg-Briand Pact, rather than the League of Nations Covenant. On the surface, this can avoid the traces of inviting the United States and Russia to assist in the implementation of pressure. However, the League of Nations is in the main position to resolve the Sino-Japanese dispute, but it does not use the Covenant, which is also difficult to understand. Recently, some people have doubted the League of Nations, saying that the Nineteen-Member Committee submitted this report to the General Assembly, and after the General Assembly passed it, it announced it to the world, or it would end it, thinking that the League of Nations had done so, it had exhausted its wisdom and ability, and from then on it would announce a stage. If so, the League of Nations would only use this empty talk of upholding justice to perfunctorily seek a way out. However, our country has lost its land and has not recovered it. Even if a negotiating committee is formed in the future according to the report, and there is no fixed deadline, and it is delayed, not only will it still not be completed, but there will be more complications. Japan is still carrying out its aggression as before. This kind of dangerous situation is by no means unexpected. Our people should urgently consider it.

On the Japanese side, although it has been under great pressure from the League of Nations, its attitude has not changed at all. It is especially determined not to relax on the issue of advancing troops to Jehol. Matsuoka replied to Drummond's advice, saying that Japan did not want to stop its military actions against Jehol. "Manchukuo" is preparing to cooperate with the Japanese army to clear all Chinese troops in Jehol Province, etc. It is obvious that it does not care about the League of Nations at all. Therefore, no matter what its attitude towards the League of Nations is today, cooperating with the puppet organization to capture Jehol is something that will be realized immediately. Whether it withdraws from the League of Nations or not, it will attack Jehol. It is not afraid of the League of Nations Covenant, and it does not care about the Nine-Power Treaty, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and all international laws. Recently, the reason why it has not moved its troops against Jehol is that it still wants to observe the situation of the League of Nations and use its means of colluding and provoking to hope to achieve some effects, help its prestige, and satisfy its greater desires. Now that it has no hope for the League of Nations, it can only simply abandon its diplomatic strategy of纵横捭阖 and devote itself to military force. Everything is free to act on its own. The diplomatic drama of the international community for a year and a half is over, and the main act of military force begins from it. May I ask who is the protagonist of this military drama, the one who fiercely fights in our country? And who is the opponent who fights against him? If we do not fight desperately, who can help me? After the failure, what position will I take? These are all things that our people should reflect on.

We discussed yesterday that after the fourth item of Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant is carried out, we have encouraged our people to make the efforts they should make in the future. The reason why we are repeatedly nagging today is that the general public still regards this new situation of the League of Nations as beneficial to us, and they are happy and comforted, and the idea of stealing peace is reborn. They do not know that under this new situation, not only can they not steal peace, but they should also work hard to rise up. Not only has the national crisis not been slightly alleviated, but it is also increasingly forced into a serious juncture. The government strictly rectifies military preparations, and all generals unite and concentrate their strength to resist this violent and strong enemy. At this time, all the people of our country should mobilize all their manpower, financial resources, and material resources to fight for the survival of our nation. Today, the North China Daily News commented on this matter, saying that the opportunity for Chinese people to help themselves has arrived. The League of Nations' advocacy of justice is only a moral victory, and success must be achieved by the entire Chinese people. Friendly countries hope that our public opinion is still like this. Why do our people stand by and not urgently seek to save themselves? The situation in Jehol is now extremely critical. May our people wake up quickly.

Full Text of the Proposal 22

(Geneva) The proposal of the nine-member sub-committee was distributed to the Nineteen-Member Committee in its final form today. The text currently released differs from the excerpt telegraphed abroad on the 12th of this month only in the arrangement of words and sentences. However, the full text contains many citations. Apart from the citations, the full text is roughly as follows:

Chapter 1 Cites Article 10 of the League of Nations Covenant, Article 2 of the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and Article 1 of the Nine-Power Treaty, and states that the League of Nations General Assembly passed the principles announced by Briand on December 10. It also states that the Administrative Council's 12th Committee invoked this principle on February 16, 1932, advising the Japanese government and declaring that any destruction of the territorial integrity of a member state of the League of Nations and changes in its political independence caused by contempt for Article 10 of the League of Nations Covenant should not be recognized by the members of the League of Nations.

The proposal then states that in order to establish a permanent understanding between China and Japan based on the above-mentioned international agreements, the resolution of the Sino-Japanese conflict must be in accordance with the following conditions of the fact-finding mission, namely the ten principles in the Lytton Report: (1) Suitable for the interests of both China and Japan, (2) Considering the interests of Soviet Russia, (3) Observing the existing treaties on all sides, (4) Recognizing Japan's interests in Manchuria, (5) Establishing new treaty relations between China and Japan, (6) Practically stipulating methods for resolving future disputes, (7) Autonomy in Manchuria (8) Internal order and security from external aggression, (9) Promoting economic coordination between China and Japan, (10) Promoting China's construction through international cooperation,

Chapter 2

Section 1 Since sovereignty over Manchuria belongs to China, the League of Nations General Assembly recommends that an agency be established in Manchuria at an appropriate time under Chinese sovereignty and suitable for the integrity of Chinese administration, endowed with extensive autonomy, and should meet legal conditions and take into account Japan's special rights, existing multilateral treaties, the rights of third parties, and the general principles and conditions contained in Chapter 1. The decision on the powers and relationship between the Chinese central government and local authorities shall be announced by the Chinese government and have international effect.

Section 2 The stationing of Japanese troops outside the South Manchurian Railway area is contrary to the legal principles that must be observed for resolving disputes. Therefore, the League of Nations General Assembly recommends the withdrawal of these troops.

The primary objective of the negotiations proposed hereinafter shall be to handle the withdrawal of troops and to decide on the conditions, stages, and deadlines for the withdrawal.

Section 3 In addition to the issues addressed in the above two proposals, the fact-finding mission's report mentions several other issues that hinder the good understanding between China and Japan, which is crucial for peace in the Far East. Therefore, the League of Nations General Assembly recommends that both parties resolve these issues based on the above-mentioned principles and conditions contained in the fact-finding mission's report.

Section 4 Negotiations necessary to implement the above proposals should be implemented, and neither party should propose conditions that are not suitable for the above proposals. Therefore, the League of Nations General Assembly recommends that both parties begin negotiations in accordance with the method prescribed below.

Please notify the Secretary-General whether each of the two parties accepts the solution proposed by the League of Nations General Assembly on the sole condition that the other party also accepts this solution. The negotiations will be held with the assistance of a committee formed by the League of Nations General Assembly in accordance with the following regulations.

The members of this committee are the signatory countries of the Nine-Power Treaty and any members of the Nineteen-Member Committee who declare their willingness to join. As soon as the Secretary-General declares that both parties have accepted the recommendations of the League of Nations General Assembly, he will appoint representatives.

The Secretary-General must also notify the United States and Russia, informing them of the acceptance of the recommendations by both parties and inviting them to send representatives to join this committee. Within one month after receiving the notification of acceptance of the recommendations from both parties, the Secretary-General must take all appropriate steps to begin negotiations. In order for the members of the League of Nations to judge whether either party is acting in accordance with the recommendations after the negotiations have begun (A) This committee should report on the progress of the negotiations, especially the negotiations on the implementation of the above-mentioned Sections 1 and 2, and in any case, it must report on the progress of Section 2 within three months after the start of the negotiations. All such reports must be sent to the League of Nations by the Secretary-General. (B) This committee may submit questions regarding the interpretation of Chapter 2 to the League of Nations General Assembly.

The League of Nations General Assembly must interpret this report under the same conditions as it was established in accordance with Section 10 of Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant.

Chapter 3 The solution currently proposed differs from the mere restoration of the original state before September 1931, and it does not allow the maintenance and recognition of the current state of Manchuria, because this kind of maintenance and recognition is not suitable for the basic principles of existing international obligations and is contrary to the good understanding between China and Japan, which is crucial for peace in the Far East.

When the members of the League of Nations pass this report, they must not take any actions that may hinder the implementation of the recommendations in this report or delay their application.

Member states will continue not to recognize the current state of Manchuria legally or in fact. Member states do not want to take any individual actions regarding the situation in Manchuria and want to cooperate with each other and, when possible, take the same actions and attitudes as non-member states concerned.

In addition, the members of the League of Nations who are signatories to the Nine-Power Treaty have promised that whenever a situation arises that, in the opinion of any signatory country, involves the application of the provisions of the Nine-Power Treaty and makes the discussion of this application appropriate, there must be full and frank contact between the signatory countries concerned.

In order to establish a situation in the Far East in accordance with the conclusions of this report to the extent possible, the Secretary-General is instructed to send a copy of this report to all countries that are not members of the League of Nations but are signatories to the Nine-Power Treaty or the Kellogg-Briand Pact, informing them of the League of Nations General Assembly's hope that they will endorse the views expressed in this report and take the same actions and attitudes as the members of the League of Nations when necessary (Reuters dispatch, 15th).

British Ministry of Commerce Releases Far East Arms Trade Figures 23

Imports to Japan Exceed Those to China

(London) Today, the British Ministry of Commerce released figures for Britain's arms trade with the Far East in 1932, showing that Japan purchased far more than China. Only in the item of small arms ammunition did China exceed Japan. The total number shipped to China was 7,735,000 rounds (excluding those shipped to Hong Kong, Macau, and leased territories). The total number shipped to Japan was 5,361,450 rounds. As for high explosives, Japan purchased a total of 490,900 rounds, while China purchased only 278,800 rounds, only half of Japan's. As for other explosives and bullets, those shipped to China were worth £1,463, while those shipped to Japan were worth £40,239, a much larger difference. As for other naval and military supplies, those purchased by Japan were worth £11,160, while those purchased by China were worth only £7,778 (National Telegraph dispatch, 15th).

Unprecedented Chaos in Japan's Six Major Metropolitan Markets 24

Stock Prices Plunge

Stock Exchanges Suspend Trading

Public Sentiment Shaken, Rumors Abound

(Tokyo) The Tokyo and Osaka stock exchanges suspended trading this afternoon due to the reactionary situation in Geneva and the sharp drop in the prices of various stocks (Reuters dispatch, 15th).

(Tokyo) Due to the situation between Japan and the League of Nations falling into a final break, the Tokyo, Nagoya, Osaka, and other major stock exchanges saw a sharp decline in the prices of various stocks in the morning session. As a result, the opening of the stock market in the afternoon session was postponed. It is reported that the Osaka Stock Exchange has decided to suspend trading temporarily. The Tokyo and Nagoya stock exchanges also stopped trading as soon as they opened. Public sentiment in the six major cities is shaken, and there are widespread rumors in the market that Japan will be subject to an economic blockade by the League of Nations after it withdraws from the League of Nations, and it is also rumored that the Japanese military will decide to declare war on China, and a Japanese-American war is inevitable. It is also said that Japanese and Russian troops have clashed somewhere, etc. The whole country is crazy, and rumors are rampant. Although the police security bureau is doing its best to crack down on rumors, it is not effective at all. It is expected that the Tokyo, Osaka, and Nagoya stock exchanges will not be able to open tomorrow morning. The inflationary boom has also left no trace of the so-called prosperous market due to the unfavorable situation of the League of Nations for Japan. The stocks that have fallen the most are those on the Tokyo Stock Exchange, among which the highest-priced stocks have fallen by about 81 yuan per share compared to the beginning of this spring. Kanebo Spinning has fallen by about 84 yuan, Japan Industries has fallen by 48 yuan, Nichiro Fisheries has fallen by more than 34 yuan, Oji Paper has fallen by about 22 yuan, and Nippon Yusen has fallen by about 11 yuan. It can be said that it is an unprecedented chaos since the founding of the stock exchange (China United Press dispatch, 15th).

More than 100,000 yuan has been repaid since then, and the principal and interest now amount to more than 400,000 yuan. Ministry of Communications Stops Anhui Construction Department from Establishing Radio Station 33

Ministry of Industry Studies Sino-Soviet Trade Treaty 34

(Nanjing) After the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and the Soviet Union, the signing of a trade treaty between the two countries is urgently needed. Since Soviet foreign trade is generally state-run, it is urgently necessary to determine whether China's trade with the Soviet Union should also be the same, in order to lay the foundation for the negotiation of the treaty. The Department of Commerce of the Ministry of Industry is currently studying this together with the Trade Treaty Review Committee. On the 15th, the ministry also consulted the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to copy and send one copy each of the trade treaties signed by the Soviet Union with the four countries of Britain, Japan, Germany, and France for reference. After the ministry has a considerable result of the research, it will invite the authorities of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Finance to discuss the matter further. According to the opinion of a certain businessman, Soviet foreign trade is all state-run, while China is a free trade country. At this time, it is difficult to implement state-run operations both theoretically and practically. The purpose of state-run operations is to adjust the surplus and deficit of production and sales and to determine appropriate prices. Currently, there is no detailed investigation of various products in China. It is not known which are surplus and which are lacking, nor is it known how much is surplus or lacking. Under these circumstances, prices cannot be determined. At the same time, other countries besides the Soviet Union freely import goods, so it is difficult to talk about adjusting surpluses and deficits. (15th Dispatch)

Measures for Soliciting Commercial Shares in Ammonium Sulfate Factory 38

Announced Yesterday by Ministry of Industry

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry has established an ammonium sulfate factory and stipulated measures for soliciting commercial shares. The Executive Yuan approved the measures on the 14th, and the Ministry of Industry announced the measures on the 15th as follows: (1) The total capital of the factory is set at 11 million yuan, of which 5 million yuan is from British and German companies or other foreign companies, 3 million yuan is from the Ministry of Industry, and 3 million yuan is invested by Chinese businessmen. (2) The factory will have shares of 100 yuan each, so the foreign side will hold 50,000 shares, and the Chinese side will hold 60,000 shares (of which 30,000 shares will be government shares and 30,000 shares will be commercial shares). (3) Chinese government shares and commercial shares will receive the same treatment for interest and dividends. (4) The right to elect directors for the Chinese government shares will be entirely exercised by representatives of the Chinese commercial shares. Half of the number of supervisors to be nominated by the Chinese side will be selected by the Minister of Industry. (5) In the event that the company suffers losses, the Chinese side will bear the losses first with government shares. If the amount exceeds the amount of government shares, the remainder will be borne by the commercial shareholders in proportion to their shareholdings. (6) When the company has profits, no government interest or dividends may be distributed until the losses have been made up. (7) When the company is established and negotiating conditions with foreign companies, three people will be appointed by the Ministry of Industry and three people will be publicly elected by the Chinese commercial shareholders to represent them. (15th Central News Agency Dispatch)

National Shock in the United States: Financial Crisis in Michigan 72

Banks Across the Country Rush to Supply Cash by Plane and Train

Reuters, Detroit, 14th - After Michigan Governor Comstock consulted with bankers and bank officials of the state overnight, he suddenly announced this morning that all banks in the state would be closed for eight days, from today until February 21st. During this period, all banks, trust companies, and financial institutions will cease operations. This is an unprecedented move in the history of Michigan. The governor stated in his announcement that this was necessary due to the state's current financial emergency. The stock exchange here is also currently closed.

National News Agency, Detroit, 14th - Today, the Union Guardian Trust Company here, due to insufficient cash to meet withdrawals from depositors and interest payments on loans from the Reconstruction Finance Corporation (RFC), with the consent of Governor Comstock and the Department of Commerce and the Treasury Department, ordered a temporary suspension of payments in Michigan for one week. All 420 state banks, 120 national banks, and the Detroit Stock Exchange in the state were closed, and the financial world turned its attention to the largest financial crisis since the economic decline. However, other well-known banks and financial institutions do not show any signs of difficulty. According to opinions from people at the Reconstruction Finance Corporation in Washington, everyone believes that this financial crisis can be resolved satisfactorily and that depositors will not suffer losses.

Causes of the Crisis 73

After the news of the suspension of payments in Michigan spread, the entire country was shocked. Stock prices on the New York and other major city stock exchanges immediately plummeted, but after learning that the crisis was largely caused by the panic of small depositors, the market rebounded slightly. Governor Comstock initially claimed that the Ford Motor Company refused to allow the company to pay small depositors and interest on RFC loans first, saying that its deposits were large and that it was the most important industry in the city, so it should have priority in payment, and therefore should be held directly responsible for causing the crisis. Later, Comstock stated that his previous statement was a misunderstanding and specifically withdrew his accusations against the Ford Motor Company, and said that the Ford Motor Company had followed the advice of Chrysler and General Motors, and continued to allocate huge sums of money to support the Union Guardian Trust Company. It has now supported 20 million yuan and promised to continue lending. In addition, the Detroit banking community also stated that it could raise 25 million yuan by tomorrow morning, and depositors could first withdraw 5% of their deposits, which greatly reduced the panic.

Congress Demands Investigation 74

The Treasury Department and the Reconstruction Finance Corporation are closely monitoring the situation here, and the Senate will also demand a thorough investigation of the contents of the loans made by the Reconstruction Finance Corporation to the borrowing banks, because rumors have spread that the company often lends huge sums of money to banks just before they are about to collapse. A proposal to investigate the company's loans has already been submitted some days ago.

Banks Across the Country Provide Assistance 75

National News Agency, Detroit, 15th - Banks across the United States today sent cash by train and plane to provide assistance to banks here, so that they could reopen as soon as possible before the end of the suspension period and resume normal operations. According to estimates from the clearinghouse here, 50 million yuan in cash has already arrived. However, there are differing opinions among financial advisors as to whether to allow banks to reopen immediately, so Governor Comstock has not yet made a decision.

Guangdong Plane Training Ends in Another Accident 85

Pilot Hu Qiyi Killed on the Spot

Air Force Headquarters Has Provided Compensation According to Precedent

Guangzhou Correspondence, the Guangdong Air Force has recently intensified training in order to cope with the national crisis. However, during diligent practice, the Morse-type No. 501 aircraft of the Fifth Squadron crashed again on the 8th. The pilot was Hu Qiyi. Hu was a captain pilot who diligently practiced his skills. A few days before the accident, he encountered danger once, but fortunately he was only slightly injured. He was hospitalized to heal his wounds, with bandages covering one eye and not yet recovered. On the 8th, he drove the plane again for training. Squadron Leader Xu Guangfu initially forbade his departure, but Hu smiled in response. He then flew the No. 501 aircraft high into the sky to practice tactics for twenty minutes. At 1:30 PM, after finishing the practice, he descended eastward, but at this time the aircraft suddenly malfunctioned, and the entire aircraft tilted and fell. Hu was unable to save the situation and eventually crashed on a low house near the Sibeidi Township in Dongshan Temple. The house collapsed and the plane was destroyed. Hu's head was pierced, blood spurted out, and he lost consciousness. Later, the Dongshangang police discovered the scene, rushed forward to rescue him, and telegraphed the Air Force Headquarters. Military doctors were immediately dispatched to provide treatment, and various medicines were injected, and the pulse began to tremble again. He was then sent to the Zhongda Hospital for rescue. After a long time, Hu's breath suddenly stopped, and he died immediately. The Air Force Department immediately provided compensation according to the precedent for death in the line of duty, purchased a coffin worth 500 yuan for a grand funeral, and approved burial in the Air Force public cemetery. Hu Qiyi was a graduate of the Fifth Class A of the Air Force School, 22 years old, and unmarried. His brother, Hu Qixuan, also died in the line of duty a few months ago while driving a plane to test the radio. The Hu brothers are the sons of Hu Hanxian, the current principal of the Aviation School. Hu has four sons who are all studying aviation, and two of them have already died. Now there are still two sons serving in the Air Force. (February 9th)

Wuxi

Finance Department Sets Deadline for Payment of Business Tax 88

County Magistrate and Business Tax Supervision Commissioner Chen Chuande received a telegram from the Finance Department yesterday, ordering that the unpaid business tax from the autumn and winter seasons of last year in all urban and rural areas under the county's jurisdiction must be paid in full by the end of February of this year. At the same time, the collection of this year's spring tax should be started immediately, and the special funds should be reported and remitted. No new or old funds should be mixed, or funds should be embezzled and remitted late, and no private loans should be made from the chamber of commerce or trade associations to make up the difference in an attempt to fulfill the task. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Chen has assisted the Business Tax Bureau in handling the matter.

Lianrong Bridge Resolved to Be Repaired 89

The Lianrong Bridge Dredging Engineering Committee, due to the loosening of the bridge foundations on both sides and the collapse of the revetments nearby, dispatched engineer Qin Xiangtao to Suzhou to invite stone mason Yu Zhenji, who built the Cuiyun Bridge in Suzhou last year, and Qianqiao Company engineer Zhu Meilin to Wuxi to inspect and make a realistic estimate. An emergency meeting was held at the County Chamber of Commerce in the afternoon on the issue of Lianrong Bridge repair. It was decided that the revetments on the east and west abutments should be demolished and rebuilt first, still in the former stone step style. The unfinished concrete work at the bottom of the bridge should be completed as soon as possible. As for whether the top of the bridge should be demolished, the person in charge of the project will inspect the situation after the revetment repair project is completed, and then discuss it further. The engineering aspect has also been contracted by contractor Jin He, with a total cost of 1,000 yuan for revetment construction on both sides of the bridge abutments, 300 yuan for setting up bridge protection wooden frames, and 50 yuan for dam protection and water monitoring. The deadline for completion is the 20th, and the dam will be opened on March 7th to allow ships to pass. The bricks, stones, lime, and other materials will be handled by the committee itself.

Changzhou

Anti-Japanese Association Inspector Assassinated 90

Huang Yixun, an inspector of the Wuyi Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, used to run a sugar warehouse, but he was unemployed after the warehouse stopped operating and was in poor circumstances. He was recommended by his colleagues to serve as an inspector in the Anti-Japanese Association, and he has been in this position for a long time. Unexpectedly, at around 8:00 AM on the 14th, a young man wearing a rush flower leather robe suddenly came to Huang's residence at No. 40 Qingguo Lane, saying that he needed to talk to Mr. Huang. At this time, Huang had just gotten up and was still wearing short clothes. He immediately went out to see him. Before he could say a few words, another young man wearing a gray leather robe broke into the room, took out a pistol from his sleeve, and fired two shots at Yixun. He also placed a letter on the table. At this time, Yixun had already fallen to the ground after being shot. The young man fired another shot at him, and then fled. Afterwards, the family reported to the nearby public security agency and carried the injured man to the Wujin Hospital for treatment. After the doctor's examination, it was found that the injuries were on the left side of the navel and the right leg, with a total of two shots. The bullets had all passed through, and because the injuries were in vital areas, he died at 11:45 AM. As for the letters left behind, one was addressed to Huang Yixun, mainly saying that he was defrauding others in the name of the Anti-Japanese Association. The second letter was addressed to all investigators of the Anti-Japanese Association, and it was a warning, signed "Sworn to Eliminate Treacherous Group Branch". Before the two young men broke into Huang's residence, Huang's friend Xie Xuanguan was at home waiting for Huang to talk. The Public Security Bureau is afraid that he is a suspect and has sent him to the County Court Procuratorate for interrogation. You Zhenji, Director of the Public Security Bureau, and Sun Fukang, Director of the First Branch, have requested punishment for their negligence in prevention.

Ningbo

Villagers Burn the Basic Cadre Team 91

The entire Sixth Squad of the Basic Cadre Team of the Cixi County Government was stationed in the Tianhou Palace at the junction of Cibei and Yaobei. Recently, due to orders to strictly prohibit flower shows, it has aroused the resentment of the villagers. At 6:00 PM on the 12th, more than 600 people, each holding weapons and flammable materials, surrounded the Tianhou Palace, forcing the entire Basic Cadre Team to withdraw empty-handed. Then they rushed into the headquarters, moved all the luggage and belongings of the Basic Cadre Team members to the open space, and set them on fire. They also searched for firearms in separate groups. They did not disperse until two hours later. After receiving the news, the County Magistrate immediately sent the Basic Cadre Brigade and police officers from the Public Security Bureau, totaling more than 50 people, fully armed, to Tianhou Palace overnight, and arrested seven ringleaders. However, the whereabouts of the Basic Cadre Squad that withdrew from Tianhou Palace are still unknown.

A Family of Four All Murdered in Revenge 92

In the Ertangtou area of Yuyao's Sixth District, a resident named Lu Songquan, who is over 40 years old, married a woman named Chen and had two sons and two daughters. The eldest son was adopted out, and the eldest daughter was married. The family still has a younger son and a younger daughter, totaling four people. However, Lu Songquan had a long-standing feud with his neighbor Lu Songxian. On the 12th, Lu Songquan went out for business and did not return at night. At about 9:00 PM the night before, Lu Songxian, carrying a pistol, suddenly entered Songquan's home and shot and killed Songquan's wife and three children at the same time. By the time the neighbors heard the alarm and rushed to chase after him, the murderer had already disappeared. At that time, the villagers saw that Songquan was not at home, so they searched in all directions, and Songquan's body was also found near the Lutangtou in the village. A family of four was all murdered in revenge, which is also very tragic.

Local News

Sudden Visit of Japanese Ambassador to Duan Qirui 93

Xu Shiying States It Was Completely Private Socializing

Absolutely No Political Involvement: Rumors Are Inaccurate

Japanese Ambassador to China, Yoshizawa Kenkichi, has been staying in Shanghai and has not met with Chinese diplomatic authorities for a long time. Recently, with the tense situation in the League of Nations, the Japanese ambassador suddenly drove to the World Academy on Ferguson Road on the morning of the day before yesterday (the 14th) at about 11:00 AM to visit Duan Qirui. He talked for about twenty minutes before leaving. This has aroused all kinds of speculation from the outside world, and some say that this is the prelude to the Japanese side's diplomatic campaign. Yesterday afternoon, the reporter of this newspaper specially visited Mr. Xu Shiying. According to Mr. Xu, the Japanese ambassador's visit to Duan was completely a private visit. When Duan came to Shanghai, Yoshizawa had already sent someone to express his regards and asked to schedule an appointment to meet and inquire about his well-being. During the meeting yesterday (i.e., the day before yesterday), the conversation only lasted twenty minutes, and most of it was ordinary socializing talk, with absolutely no political involvement. External speculation is not true. Duan's new residence on Avenue Joffre is still being renovated and will be moved into in about a week. Also, Duan's nephew, Yun Kai, told reporters from various news agencies yesterday morning that Wang Yitang is scheduled to come to Shanghai at the beginning of next month. Old Mr. Zhi's attitude has been clearly expressed, that is, patriotism has no distinction between the ruling and opposition parties. Regarding the Defense Committee, I have not heard of it. Traveling to Hangzhou will have to wait until the weather is warmer.

Support for Air Defense from All Sectors 94

The Aviation Association Held a Meeting of its Executive Committee Yesterday

The executive committee of the China Aviation Association usually meets once a week. However, for the past two weeks, due to the departures of directors Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, and Lin Wo-jiang to Hangzhou one after another, as well as the relocation of the association's offices, the meeting had been repeatedly postponed. It finally took place yesterday at 4:30 PM at the new offices on Route des Soeurs (now Route Xizang). Wang Xiaolai, Wang Zhengting, Lin Kanghou, and Lin Wo-jiang were present, while Shi Liangcai was absent. The meeting resolved several important matters, including the organizational principles for branch associations, before adjourning.

Enthusiastic Donations: The association received donations yesterday, including 300 yuan from the Shen Xin Textile Factory No. 2, saved from spring banquet expenses, and 141.87 yuan from employee donations. Additionally, employees of the Du Wu Family Cooked Meat Store on Zhejiang Road donated 30 yuan. All of these donations were delivered to the association from afar in the rain by employees of the respective factories and stores, further demonstrating the enthusiasm of all sectors for the aviation movement.

Raising Funds for a "Ningbo" Plane: The Ningbo Association in Shanghai, based on a proposal from Standing Committee members Sun Meitang and Mao Heyuan, as well as members Shui Xiangyun, Lin Bingshu, Fan Caicong, Dong Genfu, Wu Tinglun, and others, to raise funds to purchase a "Ningbo Association in Shanghai" aircraft to resist the enemy and strengthen national defense, convened a special temporary meeting of the Standing Committee yesterday to discuss implementation methods. Committee members Fang Jiaobo, Sun Meitang, Mao Heyuan, Zhang Jiguang, and others were present. Sun Meitang first explained the main purpose of the aircraft purchase proposal, and then Director Zhang Shenzhi of the association reported on the proposal plan submitted by members Shui Xiangyun and others. The matter was put to a vote, and it was decided to establish a special committee to handle the matter. The selection of committee members is scheduled for a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees on the 18th of this month to ensure careful consideration.

Raising Funds for a "Citizens' Plane": According to the Far East News Agency, the 15th District branch of the Municipal Joint Association and the joint association of businesses on Suzhou Road North, Xishan Road, and Tangjia Lane initiated a fundraising campaign for a "Citizens' Plane." Yesterday, committee members Zhu Zhichun, Liu Donghai, and Lu Rongtang sent a letter to the Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Joint Association, requesting registration to facilitate the effort. The letter stated, "The Japanese bandits are pressing, and the nation is on the verge of collapse. The only effective weapon for resisting aggression and saving the country is the air force. We are initiating a fundraising campaign for a 'Citizens' Plane' and propose the following fundraising methods: (A) Solicit aircraft donations within this district; (B) Donation registers will be issued by your association or obtained from other aviation organizations to demonstrate solemnity; (C) Daily donations will be deposited into a bank designated by your association or another aviation organization; (D) All other expenses will be borne by this association to demonstrate the intention of devoting every donation to public use; (E) Your association will appoint a committee to jointly handle the fundraising launch. We believe that saving the country is the responsibility of every citizen, and everyone is happy to contribute. Therefore, the sources and use of funds must be made public to establish credibility. We respectfully request your association to review whether these proposals are appropriate and, if approved, to register them so that we may proceed accordingly."

The Shanghai Northeast Volunteer Army Relief Association sent telegrams on the 14th of this month (the day before yesterday) to various units of the Heilongjiang forces that had retreated to Rehe, informing them of the relief efforts. Relief for the Deng Wen and Other Units: To Commanders Deng Wen, Li Zhongyi, and Shao Binshan in Rehe: After your units came to Rehe from Heilongjiang, General Zhu and Supervisor Wan sent telegrams to this association, requesting assistance. In addition to allocating 10,000 yuan in relief funds and 300,000 rounds of ammunition, which were forwarded by General Zhu, we have also allocated all the material goods raised by this association, including 90 tents, cotton uniforms, blankets, other clothing items in 96 large packages, and 13 boxes of military medical equipment purchased at the request of Messrs. Duan Zhongsen, Wu Huanzhang, and Jiang Songnian. All of these items will be transported to the front lines by Mr. Jiang Songnian for use by your units. Following recent victories in Xiuyan, Guanshanmen, and Huanghuadianzi, we blew up the South Manchurian Railway and transferred to Rehe to receive ammunition and uniforms. Three thousand iron cavalry have been fighting for over a year and are extremely weary. Please allocate 50,000 yuan in consolation money and supplies to alleviate the suffering of those who have fought bravely." Therefore, after investigating, we found that Zhang Haitian's unit had previously been allocated 100,000 rounds of ammunition and 5,000 yuan in relief funds, which were forwarded to you. Please verify whether Li Chunhua is serving as the commander-in-chief of the Second Army Corps and the squads and whether your office has provided relief, and please provide a response for verification purposes. Respectfully, the Northeast Volunteer Army Relief Association.

Reconstruction Projects in the Disaster Area 97

Actively Underway

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai Municipal Government, recognizing the importance of reconstructing the disaster area, has formulated a phased implementation plan, issuing municipal bonds worth 6 million yuan, with 4.8 million yuan actually received. The use of these funds was approved by the 215th municipal meeting on September 30th of last year. Among these uses, those directly related to the reconstruction of the disaster area include 1 million yuan for the restoration of roads and bridges in the disaster area. Other uses, such as 500,000 yuan for the restoration of roads and bridges in the old city and the completion of arterial roads, 800,000 yuan for the construction of the central area, and 500,000 yuan for the construction of roads and bridges connecting to the new railway station, are indirectly related to the reconstruction of the disaster area. It has been learned that construction has already begun on the Qingyun Bridge, Bazhi Bridge, and Tiantong'an Road Bridge, as well as the repair of Jungong Road, Zha Yin Road, and Jiaotong Road, and the completion of Pudong Avenue. Projects currently out for bid include the construction of Hongjiang Road Bridge, Linping Road Bridge, and East Jiaotong Road Bridge, as well as the laying of drainage pipes in the Wusong and Jiangwan districts. The progress of construction, with a focus on the more important projects, is briefly described below: (I) Jungong Road and Zha Yin Road: Although some repairs have been made to restore traffic since the destruction during the January 28th Incident, the road foundations are not solid and will not last. Therefore, the Bureau of Public Works has decided to add crushed brick foundations to ensure long-term stability. The total length of the two roads is 15 kilometers. Construction on Zha Yin Road has already begun and will be completed soon. Vehicles traveling from Zhabei to Wusong will be able to use this road, which will be more convenient. Construction on Jungong Road will also begin within days and is expected to be completed in three months. (II) Jiaotong Road is the only thoroughfare from Zhabei to Zhenru, and the number of vehicles traveling on it is increasing daily. Since the road has not been thoroughly repaired since the war, it is difficult to achieve perfection. The Bureau of Public Works is also adding crushed brick foundations to ensure its solidity. The road is 5 kilometers long and is expected to be completed in two months, which should bring a new look. (III) Pudong Avenue: Originally one of the city's arterial roads, the Bureau of Public Works had already begun construction, but it was halted by the January 28th Incident. Now, construction has resumed. The road is 14 kilometers long, with crushed brick foundations. All the bridges on the road are in the planning stage and will soon be under construction. Other projects, such as the repair of Baoshan Road, Qiujiang Road, Hongxing Road, and the roads and bridges in the Wusong and Jiangwan districts, are either out for bid or still in the planning stage. It is expected that these projects will also be implemented soon.

The Water Price Issue Remains in Dispute 98

The Public Works Department Held a Meeting Yesterday with No Results

The Real Estate Association Inquired but Received No Clear Answer

Tangshan Road's Sanxingfang is Cut Off from Water Again

(Public Works Department)

Board Meeting Held Yesterday: According to the Guowen News Agency, the directors of the Public Works Department held a meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss the issue of water price increases. Eleven directors were present. Due to the excessive water price increases, disputes have repeatedly arisen between the water company and residents, making it necessary to find a proper solution. Several proposals were made by the directors during the meeting and were discussed, but no decisions were made. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM, and it was decided to postpone the meeting and reconsider the issue.

Reply to Two Organizations: According to the Far East News Agency, the 26th District branch of the Municipal Joint Association and the Jiangxi Road Business Association and other organizations expressed their opposition to the installation of water meters by the British water company, which constitutes a disguised price increase, and requested the Public Works Department to stop it. Yesterday, they received a reply from the Public Works Department stating, "We have received your letter of the 8th of this month regarding the opposition to the installation of water meters. The Bureau has already forwarded this matter to the water company for proper planning to avoid increasing the burden on citizens. The matter is currently under consideration. Respectfully, the Secretariat of the Public Works Department."

(Real Estate Association)

Kui Yanfang Inquires: According to the Guowen News Agency, the Shanghai Real Estate Association received a report yesterday from Huada Real Estate Company in Shunzhi Lane, Kunming Road, stating that at noon on the 14th, Chinese and Western detectives, along with personnel from the water company, went to cut off the water. After receiving the report, Kui Yanfang, a standing committee member of the association, went to the Public Works Department at around 10:00 AM yesterday to inquire with Chief Officer Jones about which department had sent the detectives. Jones replied that he did not know about the matter. Kui then met with Superintendent Fees, who also replied that he did not know about the matter. Kui then urged him to investigate thoroughly, stating that the water price increase to 7.5 cents was still conditional and paid under protest. Now, with the installation of water meters, the price is increasing even further. He asked how landlords would be compensated for this significant loss. He stated that the water company is taking whatever it wants and cutting off the water supply, which is essential for residents' survival, at the slightest dissatisfaction, which is tantamount to holding people's lives hostage. He added that Superintendent Fees, as the superintendent of the Public Works Department and a director of the water company, should advocate for fairness and should not prioritize the interests of a small number of people in the water company over the interests of the majority of the public.

(Tenants)

According to the Guowen News Agency, since the water company installed new water meters, water cutoffs have been frequent. Yesterday, Sanxingfang on Tangshan Road was cut off from water again. Tenants negotiated with the Public Works Department and the water company but received no clear answers. The details are as follows:

Petition to the Ratepayers Association: At around 11:00 AM yesterday, the British water company suddenly sent a Westerner and several workers to close all the water supply in Sanxingfang on Tangshan Road, effectively cutting off the water supply. The tenants of the neighborhood, believing that water is an indispensable part of daily life and that the sudden lack of water would endanger their lives, elected Zhu Xingfu, Fang Mingcai, Pan Zheming, Peng Zizhen, Wang Yaozeng, Zhang Defu, and others to rush to the Chinese Ratepayers Association to petition. They were received by Secretary Tao Leqin. The representatives were agitated and demanded that the Ratepayers Association immediately negotiate strongly with the Public Works Department and order the water company to restore the water supply. Secretary Tao drafted a letter of introduction for the representatives to meet with Counselor He DeKui at the Public Works Department and then introduce them to meet with Superintendent Jones for a response. The representatives thanked him after receiving the letter and went to the Public Works Department to negotiate.

Negotiations with the Public Works Department: The representatives went directly to the Public Works Department to negotiate. The Counselor received them and conveyed the representatives' petition to the Superintendent. The Superintendent used the telephone to inquire with the water company, which replied that the water was cut off because the landlord had not paid the fees. The representatives then presented their previous payment checks. The Superintendent then asked the representatives to negotiate directly with the water company. The representatives received no clear answer and then went to the water company to negotiate, but there were no results. It is reported that the tenants felt that the Public Works Department had failed to ensure the stability of important issues for the public within the settlement and were extremely dissatisfied. They may take further steps.

Water Prices Increased Threefold: The neighborhood consists of 107 buildings, with hundreds of households and over a thousand residents. Since the water was cut off, people have been panicking. The property is owned by the Jingji Company. After the water company installed water meters without authorization, the company believed that the matter was still under negotiation and continued to pay the water price at the previous rate of 7.5 cents. They sent two checks, No. 0032243 for 1,000 yuan from the Zhejiang Industrial Bank and No. 454610 for 666.20 yuan from the Zhongfu Bank, on December 1st of last year. However, the water company ignored the social situation and returned the two checks. They then resent them on January 24th, but they were returned again. The water company also limited the Jingji Company to pay the increased water price by February 3rd, or the water would be cut off. Although the Jingji Company negotiated with the water company several times, the water was finally cut off yesterday morning. The British water company claimed that the water was cut off because the landlord did not pay the water bill, which is a fabrication. At the same time, the water company's tough attitude is evident. Since the installation of the meters, the amount of the water price increase is more than threefold.

Public Security Bureau and Other Agencies Jointly Announce Standards for Rent Reduction and Exemption in the War Zone 105

The city suffered great losses during the January 28th Incident. The Municipal Government sent personnel from various bureaus to conduct on-site surveys and propose four standards for rent reduction and exemption, which have been approved. Yesterday, the Public Security, Finance, Land, and Social Bureaus jointly announced, "Regarding the joint announcement, this bureau and others previously received Instruction No. 3017 from the Municipal Government, stating that, according to the petition from war-zone merchants Chen Xianshen and others, they suffered great losses last year due to the war and requested rent reduction and exemption. The instruction ordered us to jointly review and report. After several discussions and on-site surveys, and in reference to the standards for rent reduction and exemption in the war zone, we proposed four standards for rent reduction and exemption in the war zone and submitted them to the Municipal Government for approval. Now, we have received Instruction No. 34836 from the Municipal Government, stating, 'The submission has been noted. As various bureaus have sent personnel to conduct on-site surveys and assess the disaster situation and propose reduction and exemption standards, which are appropriate, they should be implemented as proposed. The bureaus should jointly announce and post the standards in the area for public awareness.' Therefore, we are now announcing the four rent reduction and exemption standards as follows, and we urge the public in the area to comply with them. The announcement includes: (I) For houses that have not been destroyed, rent exemption for three months in accordance with the rent reduction and exemption standards; (II) For houses that have been destroyed but have now been restored or partially restored, rent exemption for six months; (III) For houses that have been destroyed and not restored, but the surrounding area has commercial activity, rent exemption for nine months; (IV) For houses that have been destroyed and not restored, and the surrounding area has not been restored, rent exemption for one year."

Prohibition of Free Levying of Contributions by Organizations 106

The Municipal Government Received Instructions from the Executive Yuan Yesterday to Comply

The Municipal Government received instructions from the Executive Yuan yesterday, stating that the free levying of contributions by people's organizations not only causes people to doubt mass organizations and hinders their own development but also inevitably disrupts social order and violates national laws and regulations. All such activities should be prohibited. The full text of the instructions is recorded below for compliance. "The Ministry of Interior has reported that, after reviewing the various proposals decided at the Second National Interior Affairs Conference, all those that could be adopted have been reported or circulated. The proposal from the Fujian Provincial Department of Civil Affairs to prohibit mass organizations from levying contributions was approved by the conference and submitted to the Executive Yuan for prohibition. After further review, the Ministry believes that the free levying of contributions by mass organizations will disrupt the national financial system and increase the burden on the people. If not strictly prohibited, it will not only cause people to doubt mass organizations and hinder their own development but also inevitably disrupt social order and violate national laws and regulations. Therefore, we are submitting the original proposal for your review and implementation for public convenience. In addition to issuing instructions and circulating them, we are also submitting the original proposal and ordering the Municipal Government to comply, instructing its subordinates to prohibit all such activities."

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends Telegram Requesting Rectification of the Excise Tax on Machine-Made Goods 107

Telegram to the Ministry of Finance

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, requesting rectification of the tax exemption method for machine-made goods. The original telegram stated, "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: On the 13th of this month, the Shanghai Chinese Soap Industry Association sent a letter stating that, 'We have received a letter from your association stating that, in response to our previous request to the Ministry of Finance to order that machine-made goods approved for machine-made treatment be exempt from tax in the same way as native goods, the Ministry has approved that machine-made goods transported domestically by sailing vessels or trains, which were originally taxed by the Customs, should continue to be exempt from tax, so as to be treated the same as native cloth.' We have informed our members, the machine-made soap factories. Now, the Nanyang Soap Factory and others have reported that they have complied with the Ministry's approval. However, according to the Customs, the exemption for machine-made goods refers to factories that are not registered with the Ministry. Factories that were previously registered with the Ministry and approved do not have explicit exemption statements in the original approval and must still pay taxes before they can be released.' Our members, including Wuzhou Guben, Nanyang, Xinchang, Henry, Dingfeng, Yonghe, Lida, Shouhua, Huachang, Gongmao, and Qixin factories, are all registered with the Ministry and are approved to receive machine-made goods treatment. Therefore, our previous letter stated that we had received approval on record. Now, the Customs is insisting on its position, which is a misunderstanding. The machine-made goods treatment embodies prudence in promotion. Therefore, registration is necessary to have this legal status. The original approval clearly refers to machine-made goods, which of course have gone through registration procedures. Otherwise, how can they be considered machine-made goods? Now, registered machine-made goods cannot be treated the same as goods that claim to be machine-made without approval, which is unfair. Therefore, we respectfully request your association to request the Ministry of Finance to inform the Customs again to avoid unfairness.' We have investigated that the tax exemption method for machine-made goods imitating foreign styles is based on registration approval. Those not registered with the Ministry are taxed as native goods, which has been the case for a long time. Now, the Customs is saying that those not registered with the Ministry can enjoy tax-exempt treatment, while factories that have been registered with the Ministry must still pay taxes for release. We do not know what regulations this claim is based on, which is difficult to understand. We respectfully request your Ministry to review the situation, issue an order to the Customs to rectify the situation, and order them to handle the matter according to the previous approval to show fairness, which would be greatly appreciated. Respectfully, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Sugar Industry and Southern Goods Industry Dispute: Municipal Chamber of Commerce to Mediate Today 110

Yesterday, Comparison Weighing Between Northern Goods and Southern Goods Industries

United Market to Hold General Meeting Tomorrow

The Shanghai Sugar, Northern Goods, and Southern Miscellaneous Goods Joint Market has been experiencing a dispute between the sugar and northern goods industries and the southern goods industry regarding the conversion rates for the new weighing instruments. Yesterday, the two sides conducted a comparison weighing. This afternoon, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce will convene a meeting to mediate. Details are as follows:

Yesterday's Comparison Weighing: Representatives from the northern goods industry and the southern goods industry conducted a comparison weighing at 3:00 PM yesterday at the Kunyuan Northern Goods Company on Foreign Firm Street in the French Concession, using the old system guildhall scales and the new system municipal scales. Attendees included Gong Jingyan and Ni Baofu from the Southern Goods Industry Association, and Qiu Yangzhi from the Northern Goods Industry Association. The results of the comparison weighing showed that 100 catties on the new municipal scales equaled 97.25 catties on the old system guildhall scales. Calculating at a 90% discount, this equals 87.525, which differs from 88 by 0.475, and from 87 by 0.525. However, the southern goods industry still demands 87, while the northern goods industry insists on 88.

Today's Mediation: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce is scheduled to convene a meeting at 2:00 PM this afternoon, bringing together the Sugar Industry Association, the Northern Goods Industry Association, and the Southern Goods Industry Association in the Municipal Chamber of Commerce meeting room to mediate and decide on a fair conversion method. Luo Qinghua has been designated as the chairman. Zheng Zenan and Xu Jingfu will represent the sugar industry, Qiu Yangzhi will represent the northern goods industry, and Gong Jingyan and Ni Baofu will represent the southern goods industry.

Market Meeting: A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency met with Qiu Yangzhi of the Northern Goods Industry Association yesterday. According to Qiu, the conversion rate for the new weighing instruments is based on a resolution passed by the Joint Market. Without approval from a general meeting, it cannot be changed without authorization. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce has scheduled a mediation for the 16th. As for the Joint Market, it has been decided to convene the executive committee again on the 17th to discuss the policy.

However, the number of overseas Chinese in Finland is small, and this embassy has now received an order from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to close down and is in the process of finalizing matters. Overseas Chinese in Chicago Donate Large Sum to Volunteer Army 113

Overseas Chinese in Chicago, deeply angered by the Japanese invaders' barbarity, their invasion of the Northeast, and their recent seizure of Shanhaiguan and Jiuguan, constantly advancing and acting unscrupulously, formed the Chicago Branch of the Chinese Nationalist Party, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Donation Committee, and the Chicago Chinese Consolidated Benevolent Association Theater Troupe to raise funds through performances to support the brave soldiers fighting the enemy. Now that the performances have concluded, a meeting has been convened and it was resolved that the Bank of China would remit 10,000 yuan in national currency to the Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe Volunteer Army Support Association for distribution to the various anti-Japanese volunteer armies in the Northeast. The remaining amount will be made up by Tan Zan. On the 21st of last month, Tan Zan, Zheng Junze, Wu Liu, and Xie Weibang were appointed to handle the remittance to Shanghai. The original text of the association's official letter is transcribed below:

Letter to the Support Association: "We write to inform you that the brutal Japanese are acting with violence and causing disaster in our country. The Northeast has been lost for more than a year, and the 30 million compatriots outside the Pass are suffering terribly. Since the 'September 18th' incident of the previous year, the Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe National Salvation Volunteer Army have been fighting the enemy and striving for the glory of our Chinese nation. Their brave spirit is enough to encourage the weak, but they suffer from weapons fire, hunger, cold, and disease. Their situation is extremely difficult, with supplies and weapons cut off. How can they endure? If the Northeast falls, the interior will also fall. Now that Shanhaiguan has been lost and Rehe is in danger, the Northeast Volunteer Army is isolated outside the Pass. If we want them to reinforce each other and attack the Japanese, the rear must provide support. The entire nation has a responsibility. Only iron and blood can win survival, and only money can speak to strength. Material and spiritual assistance must complement each other. This will not only boost the morale of the army but also inspire the spirit of the people to fight together, resist the enemy, and save the nation, showing our determination to resist to the end. Our association was formed at the beginning of the Shanghai war last year and has remitted funds to support the army, as reported previously. In order to meet the urgent needs of the Northeast Volunteer Army, we have joined forces with the Chicago Chinese Consolidated Benevolent Association Theater Troupe to raise more funds for support. We are remitting 10,000 yuan through the Shanghai Bank of China today. The draft is enclosed with this letter. Please cash it and hand it over to your association. In correspondence with your receipt, please send it to the front for distribution to the anti-Japanese volunteer army in Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe, in the hopes that this will provide some comfort. This small amount of money is the hard-earned sweat of our overseas Chinese. We will continue to work hard to provide long-term assistance. Please verify receipt of the aforementioned remittance, and promptly send us a receipt for verification."

Letter to the Bank of China: "We write to inform you that we are remitting 10,000 Shanghai dollars through your bank. Please verify receipt, cash the draft, and send it to the Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe Volunteer Army Support Association in Shanghai for use in supporting the anti-Japanese volunteer army fighting in the four northeastern provinces. Please obtain a receipt from the Support Association and send it to us for verification."

Inquiry into Shao Wansheng Labor Dispute Yesterday 117

Party and Government Agencies Schedule Mediation

Following the labor dispute due to the dismissal of workers at Shao Wansheng in the local southern goods industry, the Party and government agencies have mediated several times without success. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, the Social Affairs Bureau convened another inquiry. However, because the industry association did not attend, only Shao Yuqing and Wang Xingzhai, managers of Shao Wansheng, Yu Yaoqiu, Fan Xinsheng, and Shan Mengsheng, labor union representatives, and Dai Youheng, a representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, were present. Zhu Chongtao, a mediator from the Social Affairs Bureau, chaired the meeting. He stated that this case has been mediated several times, but no resolution has been reached due to differing opinions between the two parties. He hoped that each side would make concessions. The labor representatives stated that the employer had no reason to dismiss the two workers and demanded that they all be reinstated. The employer stated that the previous owner was from Ningbo, and this time the owner is from Shaoxing, leading to some Ningbo workers not being hired. The chairman believed that the employer's reasons were insufficient and that the workers should be allowed to return to work. The employer agreed to consult and reply within three days. The Party and government agencies announced that a scheduled mediation would be held again.
