British Constable Charged with Forgery 123

Barker, a Briton who previously served as a probationary constable in the Public Concession's Third District, was arrested at his home at 222 Huanlong Road at 10:00 AM yesterday (the 14th) on charges of forgery. At the time, Deputy Detective Crawford and Lind of the British Consular Police, together with the French Concession police, went to arrest him. He was taken back to the General Police Station and sent to the British Police Court. After questioning about the circumstances of the arrest, the hearing will continue this morning (the 15th). Barker pleaded not guilty and will hire a lawyer to defend him. According to the police, Barker forged a promissory note dated October 11th of last year, imitating the signatures of Harrison and Mahon, two probationary constables in the Third District. Barker previously served in the military and joined the police force when the army left Shanghai. He quit one month ago.

Zheng Xitang's Condition Gradually Improving 124

Recovery Expected in Two to Three Weeks

Zheng Xitang, a prominent figure in the shipping industry, was suddenly attacked by kidnappers at the entrance of the Pingan Shipping Company on Xintai Wharf in Nanshi at around 1:00 PM on the 11th of this month. Zheng resisted strongly and escaped, but a bullet fired by the bandits killed Zheng's bodyguard, a Russian named Saishuofu. Zheng's forehead was also wounded by the gunfire. The bandits also fired shots to resist arrest, wounding two police officers and a pedestrian, who were taken to Tongren Hospital for treatment. These details have been reported in detail in this newspaper. It is now known that Zheng, after entering Tongren Hospital, was examined by Western doctors who found that he was only wounded by a bullet in the left posterior skull and that his brain was not injured. Therefore, the Western doctors removed the broken skull fragments during surgery, applied medication, and allowed him to sleep peacefully. Yesterday was the fourth day and he has passed the danger period, progressing well. His temperature has not increased, and he is mentally clear, able to consume thin porridge and milk. His life is expected to be saved. However, the wound is painful, and the Western doctor insisted that he could not receive visitors or talk too much to avoid overexerting himself. Therefore, business figures who visited the hospital in recent days were received and dealt with by his secretary, Xu Wanli. It is expected that Zheng's wound will recover in about two to three weeks, and he will be discharged from the hospital. Zheng has ordered that 400 yuan be given for the funeral expenses of the body of Zheng's bodyguard, the Russian Saishuofu, which was claimed by Jigu Jinuo (the nephew of the Russian) who took possession of the body and coffin.

The Long Arm of the Law Snares Arch-Bandit Fang Jin-hong's Killer 126

Jiang Fuquan Lingers in the Courthouse Courtyard

Identified by Accomplices Ding Zinan and Others

The Arresting Officer Ordered Him Detained for Further Investigation

Fang Jin-hong, the import department head of the Sincere Company, was shot and killed on Yu Yuan Road in Western Shanghai around 8:00 PM on December 9th of last year by a group of bandits from Tongzhou, including Ding Zinan, Zhang Qishan, Zhang A'er, Yu Afu, Tang Yongfu, Qian Hengshan, Xi Houtao, and Wu A'er, in a kidnapping attempt that went awry. Subsequently, the detective division of the Mixed Court Police discovered that the bandits were hiding in Changping Road and the French Concession, and arrested them. The case was heard by Judge Wu Tingqi of the First Special District Court, who sentenced Ding Zinan and others to death, and Yu Afu and others to life imprisonment. Recently, the police learned that the key suspect in the case, Cao Houfu, was hiding on Longjiang Road, and ordered detectives to arrest Cao and bring him to the First Special District Court, requesting that he be detained for investigation. All of these details have been reported in the newspapers. Yesterday morning was the scheduled hearing. In addition to bringing Cao to court, the police also escorted Ding Zinan and others from the Western Prison to testify. When Ding Zinan and the others passed through the courthouse courtyard, they caught sight of Jiang Fuquan and shouted that he was their accomplice. The detectives then stepped forward, arrested Jiang, and brought him to the case. Judge Qian Wenji took the bench in the Eighth Tribunal to hear the case. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang presented the case, stating that the detectives were escorting Ding Zinan, who had already been sentenced to death, to the court, when Ding and others shouted, saying that Jiang Fuquan was involved in the kidnapping of Fang Jin-hong, and that he was immediately arrested. He requested that the court question Jiang and allow him to be taken back to the police station for investigation. Ding Zinan then testified that he had been introduced to Jiang Fuquan by his accomplice Zhang Qishan, and that Jiang Bao was involved in the kidnapping. The judge then questioned Jiang Fuquan, who stated that he was 38 years old, from Tongzhou, living at 980 Jiaojianshi Road, and ran a small car business. He stated that last December, when the police arrested Ding Zinan and others, he had gone to help, and that they were falsely accusing him out of spite. The judge considered the testimony and ordered that Jiang Fuquan be taken back to the police station for investigation.

Young Woman Suspected of Being a Thief 127

A Slight Seduction Could Get Her Into a Hotel

Secretly Followed All the Way to Her Home

Yesterday morning around 10:00 AM, two men brought a young woman to the Second Precinct of the First District, accusing her of theft and requesting that she be punished. The woman was quite beautiful, especially her pair of limpid eyes, clear and bright, set beneath delicate eyebrows, enough to captivate a man's soul and make him feel distracted. She also had a graceful figure and wore a dark blue woolen serge, fur-lined cheongsam, a fur coat, and high-heeled leather shoes, making it clear at first glance that she was a modern, seductive woman. During the preliminary hearing by the precinct chief, one man, Qiu Xitao, 31 years old, from Baoshan, residing at No. 9 Fuchang Lane, Xiaodongmen, stated that the other man, Sun Weishen, was his housemate. He continued, "Around 9:00 AM this morning, the woman (pointing to the young woman) secretly entered my home. I caught a glimpse of her acting suspiciously. However, because she was dressed in fashionable clothes, like someone from the upper class, I did not dare to scold her. I asked her what she was doing there, and she said she was looking for a friend. I told her to wait a moment, and then gathered my housemate Sun Weishen and others, and we searched each room to see if anything was missing. Sun discovered that a gold ring, engraved with his name, Weishen, was missing. It had been placed in a leather wallet, hidden in a box. We then searched the woman, and found Sun's gold ring inside her glove. At this point, the stolen goods were found, and we realized that the beautiful young woman was in fact a thief. Therefore, we brought her here, requesting that you investigate." He then presented the stolen ring. Sun Weishen testified that he was 30 years old, from Zhenhai, and worked as an accountant at a Shenzhuang (silk firm). The rest of his statement was the same as Qiu's. When questioned, the young woman stated that her name was Zhang Xiuying, 22 years old, from Hubei. Her husband used to be a battalion commander under a certain division, but unfortunately died in battle during a certain war. She is now staying with a relative near the Grand Clock in the French Concession. She continued, "Last night, after dinner, I went to the Tianyun Tower amusement park in the Wing On Company. I happened to meet this man (pointing to Sun Weishen). He immediately came over and started flirting with me. I was bewitched, and after the show ended, he took me to a nearby hotel and rented a room for three dollars and change. That night, I was raped. Afterwards, because my body was defiled, I told him that I wanted to stay with him for life. Sun agreed and suggested we exchange gold rings as a sign of our commitment. I gave him a gold ring engraved with the words 'Beloved,' and he gave me a ring engraved with his name. Today, when I said goodbye, I wanted to follow him to see what his home was like, so I secretly followed him. However, his friend noticed me and suspected me of stealing, and Sun suddenly turned on me, falsely accusing me of being a thief and taking the gold ring he had given me off my finger, claiming it as stolen property. I never expected such ingratitude." Because the statements of both parties differed, it was ordered that a written report be prepared and sent to the bureau for investigation.

The Plan Has Been Submitted to the Ministry of Railways

Implementation Expected This Spring

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railway lines pass through many scenic areas. Tourists flock to these areas in the spring and autumn. It has been learned that the two railway bureaus have already contacted the China Travel Service and have drafted detailed implementation plans, as well as tour budgets for Hangzhou, Suzhou, Wuxi, and other places, detailing special train ticket prices, departure times, train organization, tour programs, etc., and submitted them to the ministry for review. It is currently under review and research. It is rumored that the special train service may be implemented this spring. (Daily News)

Song Park Road to Be Widened 129

To Connect with Tibet Road, Forming a Thoroughfare

With the relocation of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway North Station imminent, the Municipal Bureau of Public Works had planned to widen the section of Song Park Road from Xinjiang Road to Zhongxing Road, in order to connect it with Tibet Road and facilitate traffic. It has now been learned that this widening plan has been approved by the Municipal Council and the Municipal Assembly, and a deadline of April 15th of this year has been set for the demolition of roadside buildings that obstruct the road, in order to begin construction. The announcement jointly issued by the Land Bureau and the Public Works Bureau is transcribed below:

Announcement:

Considering that the North Station of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway is about to be relocated, and in order to facilitate traffic, this Bureau of Public Works had planned to widen the section of Song Park Road connecting to Tibet Road, from Xinjiang Road to Zhongxing Road. In November of last year, a road map was drawn up and submitted to the Municipal Government, which was approved by the Municipal Council, and a deadline of April 15th of this year was set for the demolition of roadside buildings that obstruct the road. In addition to this Bureau of Land Affairs collecting land according to the city's road construction levy regulations, and this Bureau of Public Works preparing for construction, this announcement, along with the attached road map and instructions, is hereby promulgated for public knowledge.

17-Year-Old Youthful Robber Xiao Tinggui Sentenced 130

To Six Years of Imprisonment

Xiao Tinggui, a 17-year-old local youth, on the evening of the 12th of last month at 8:00 PM, gathered a group of accomplices and, armed with weapons, robbed the home of Sun Lu, a woman from Shaoxing, at the entrance of the Shenxing Lane pedestrian overpass on Minquan Road in the French Concession. Xiao opened fire to resist arrest and show off his power, wounding the left hand of the victim, Guan Qi Liang Linxi. Liang blew a police whistle, and the robbers, hearing the sound, climbed over the wall and fled. Xiao was captured by the victim and his handgun was seized. Detectives from the French Concession police rushed to the scene and arrested Xiao. It was discovered that on the same morning, he and his accomplices had robbed the home of Qian Haoliang at No. 20 Yinhe Lane, Fangbang Bridge, and on the 4th of the same month, he and his accomplices had robbed the home of Yang Asi at No. 122 Wangzhi Road. The robbery of Sun Lu's home was instigated by Yang Xiaosanzi, who lived with Lu, Yang and Zhang Zijin, who received the stolen goods, were also arrested and sent to the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer charged the defendants with robbery, assault, conspiracy to commit robbery, and receiving stolen goods. The trial has concluded, and yesterday afternoon, Judge Li Changnian presided over the First Criminal Court and sentenced Xiao Tinggui to four years of imprisonment for each of the three counts of armed robbery with three or more accomplices, to be served concurrently for a total of six years. Yang Xiaosanzi was sentenced to one year of imprisonment for conspiracy to commit robbery, and Zhang Zijin was sentenced to two months of imprisonment for receiving stolen goods. The handgun was confiscated. After the sentencing, the defendants were transferred to the detention center to await the expiration of the appeal period before being sent to prison.

Reader's Advisor

Sympathy for Mr. Ren Wangyue's View on Suicide 138

[Letter from Mr. Zhu Cixun]

After reading Mr. (your name here) answer to Ren Wangyue, as asked on the fifth of this month, "Is my view on suicide correct?", I feel that Mr. (your name here)'s thinking is a bit aristocratic. He (you) has (have) not considered the pain of the suicidal, and is(are) completely standing(ing) from the position of an upper-class level to sing high-pitchedly! I believe that suicide is certainly not the upward psychology of human beings, but we must think about the motives of suicide, and fundamentally attribute it to the shortcomings of the social system. Like the first type of suicide that Mr. Ren mentioned, the reason for Mr. (your name here) objection is: "As long as a person has a sound mind and thinking, even if he is blind, deaf, or lame, he has his work effectiveness, and he has the opportunity to do his best for society. If he commits suicide because of his unhealthy body and weakness, to be honest, half of the Chinese people will commit suicide." This reason is certainly not bad, but I want to ask Mr. (your name here) whether a sound mind and thinking must have considerable cultivation? Does the method of this cultivation still require the strength of society to create it? Second, blind people, deaf people, and lame people can all do their best for society, but how can they do their best? Do they have the opportunity to do their best? Last year, I personally saw a helpless disabled person who could not enter the disabled home to request support. The reason for the disabled home's refusal was that the number of people exceeded the quota. Ask this kind of disabled person, how should he struggle? The second type of suicide that Mr. Ren mentioned, the reason for Mr. (your name here) objection is: "The life of a dark slave is formed by the dark forces that oppress society and unequal society. To break this dark force, it is necessary to combine the greatest and most determined revolutionary forces in society, and accumulate the most lasting and valuable experience of struggle, and support a very strong and stable war organization to achieve success." The words are right, but, I think, people who live in slavery, if they have the spirit, perseverance, and courage that Mr. (your name here) mentioned above, then they would have gotten rid of their slave life long ago. Mr. (your name here), you must know that the life of a dark slave does indeed have the desire to resist and break through as Mr. Ren said, but it is impossible!" I think that people who live a dark slave life who cannot break free, if they have the courage to commit suicide, it may not be a bloody revolution. According to the current ban on keeping slaves promulgated by the government, does this mean that there are no slaves in China? If an underage girl is bought by someone to be a maid, ask her how to resist, how to break through her dark slave life? In addition, the environment created by bad customs and habits, I can responsibly say that she will never get sympathy and help from others, because many, many people commit suicide because they cannot bear the pain of this inhuman life. We cannot say that this kind of suicide is the most thorough act of unconditional surrender of a slave to his master. We can only attribute it to the shortcomings of the social system. Moreover, the actions of resistance and breakthrough are not that simple in fact. Like President Abraham Lincoln's emancipation of black slaves in the United States, he went through many difficulties. The emancipated black slaves still felt the pain of having nowhere to go for a while. Therefore, to resist and break through the dark slave life, it does not rely on the power of individuals to do it well.

Like the third type of suicide that Mr. Ren mentioned, the reason for Mr. (your name here) objection is: "What kind of learning and talents does Mr. Ren have that can arouse people's sympathy, and be worthy of a high carriage and fat horses, rich clothes and good food, a proud wife and beautiful concubines to solve Mr. Ren's depression and emptiness." The reason is very sufficient. We are not conceited now, nor are we blaming others. There are people in the current society who have less learning and talent than us who are eating their salary without doing anything and occupying a superior position. There may not be such people, to be rude, if someone like Mr. reporter is not considered a talent, nor can he be said to be a mediocre talent; if you lose your job and suffer from poverty, your job will be taken away by a mediocre talent who can flatter others, then, Mr. (your name here), please tell me sincerely, are you optimistic or not? Are you depressed or not? When you get to that situation, I am afraid that the number of people who sympathize with you will be reduced, and you can only curse the shortcomings of the social system? If you are in such a situation, and there is still a good way to struggle, please tell me in detail! Then people with high learning and talents who cannot get the opportunity to make progress in their lives will have to respect you as the leader of the social group. We are not trying to learn the Stoic school of Greece to advocate suicide. I have also painted a few articles about the voices of the weak and the troubles of young people, my outlook on life; but I always conclude with improving the social system; suicide is not necessarily a sign of the weak. Therefore, in the current society where there is no order, there is a crisis of suicide everywhere. To save this crisis, we must try to improve the social system. How to work hard to improve, I dare not say. Mr. (your name here) cannot advocate suicide. What we hope from Mr. (your name here) is what methods there are to eliminate suicide? The question is getting further and further away, and the scope is also expanding, so I will stop writing here. If Mr. (your name here) thinks it is worth discussing, we will discuss it in the Reader's Advisor column. (Reply will be published tomorrow)

Regulations for National Construction Scholarships Jointly Organized by the Examination and Education Ministries 140

Dai Chuanxian, President of the Examination Yuan, has initiated a National Construction Scholarship Committee jointly organized by the Examination and Education Ministries to promote academics and advance national construction. The summary of the regulations is as follows:

(Organization of the Scholarship Committee) The committee will have three presidents, with the President of the Examination Yuan as an ex-officio president. The other two will be appointed by the National Government. There will be one chairman, rotating annually between the Chairman of the Examination Commission and the Minister of Education, and one vice-chairman, rotating annually between the Vice-Chairman of the Examination Commission and the Vice-Minister of Education. The Examination Commission and the Ministry of Education will appoint several committee members, five to seven of whom will be standing committee members, designated by the chairman, with a term of three years. However, additional reviewers and assistant reviewers may be temporarily appointed as needed for each examination or review to focus on evaluation, including determining the scope of questions, evaluation criteria, review of writings, deciding on passing grades, the total amount of scholarships, the amount of individual scholarships, the number and types of awards and certificates, and fundraising. All matters must be decided in meetings chaired in rotation by the presidents. The scholarship scope is roughly divided into two categories: (1) essays deemed excellent after evaluation and (2) academic works deemed truly valuable after review. Those who apply for essay examinations must meet the following requirements: (1) government employees with proof of employment, (2) non-incumbent government employees who are qualified to take the higher examinations and have proof from two incumbent recommended-rank or higher government officials or equivalent party affairs personnel, or presidents of specialized schools or above, and (3) those with equivalent academic qualifications and proof from higher academic institutions or academic organizations. Academic works must be recommended by national academic institutions, national universities, or academic organizations with achievements. After passing the review, rewards will be given. The scholarship award methods for essay examinations are: (1) awarding scholarships, with the total annual scholarship amount limited to 10,000 yuan each time, the total quarterly scholarship amount limited to 3,000 yuan each time, and the total monthly scholarship amount limited to 1,000 yuan each time, (2) awarding medals and certificates, with the number of people and types of awards and certificates to be determined by the committee and submitted to the Examination Yuan for approval. The committee's fundraising includes: (1) government allocations, (2) donations from private individuals and public organizations, (3) interest on deposits, and (4) proceeds from publications. A fund management committee will be established, composed of representatives from the Executive Yuan, Legislative Yuan, Judicial Yuan, Examination Yuan, Control Yuan, Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics, and the Central Bank, with each institution sending one representative. Those who donate more than 10,000 yuan but less than 1,000 yuan may publicly elect one to seven representatives to participate in management. The committee members will each form a group, and each group will elect one standing committee member to form a standing committee to handle committee affairs.

(Regulations for Essay Examinations) The draft regulations for scholarship essay examinations have been drafted as follows: Article 1: These regulations are based on Article 8 of the Regulations for the National Construction Scholarship Committee. Article 2: The examination periods of the committee are as follows: (1) Annual examinations will be held once a year in March. (2) Quarterly examinations will be held four times a year in spring, autumn, and winter. (3) Monthly examinations will be held once a year. If the examination period cannot be held as scheduled due to special circumstances, the National Construction Scholarship Committee may decide to temporarily change it in a meeting. Article 3: The examination dates, subject categories, submission locations, number of admissions, and scholarship amounts for each examination in the preceding article will be announced by the National Construction Scholarship Committee two weeks before each examination. Article 4: Annual examinations are divided into two tests: the first test is a free essay written outside the examination hall, with a time limit of two weeks; the second test is an in-person interview, with a time limit of one day. Those who are not admitted in the first test may not take the second test. Quarterly and monthly examinations each consist of one test, both of which are free essays written outside the examination hall. The quarterly examination has a time limit of three days, and the monthly examination has a time limit of one day. Article 5: When holding the second test of the annual examination, the Control Yuan should be requested to send personnel to supervise the examination. Article 6: Examinees should pay an examination fee when registering for the examination and receiving the examination paper. The annual examination fee is two yuan per paper, the quarterly examination fee is one yuan per paper, and the monthly examination fee is five jiao per paper. Article 7: The personnel setting the questions for each examination should strictly maintain confidentiality and not disclose them to the outside world before the examination period. Article 8: The examination questions for each examination will be announced in front of the Examination Commission and the Ministry of Education and published in major newspapers in and outside the capital. However, the examination questions for the second test of the annual examination should be issued temporarily inside the examination hall. Article 9: Examinees should submit the examination papers within the time limit announced for each examination. Papers submitted after the deadline will not be accepted. Article 10: Examinees for the second test of the annual examination should enter the examination hall on time. Those who arrive after the deadline will not be allowed to take a make-up test. Article 11: The evaluation procedures for each examination are as follows: (1) For the annual examination, the assistant reviewers will conduct the initial review and propose scores, the reviewers will conduct the second review and determine scores, and the presidents will conduct the final review and determine scores. (2) For the quarterly examination, the assistant reviewers will conduct the initial review and propose scores, the reviewers will conduct the second review and determine scores, and the chairman will conduct the final review and determine scores. (3) For the monthly examination, the reviewers will conduct the review and determine scores, and the chairman will conduct the final review and determine scores. Article 12: After the examination papers of each examination have been evaluated, the number of admissions and the scholarship amount for each person will be announced in addition to being posted. Article 13: The scholarship amount to be awarded for the admitted examination papers will be given separately according to the amount specified in the announcement. If there are special works, the presidents may increase the amount to show excellence. Article 14: The top five candidates admitted in the annual examination, or the top five candidates successively admitted in the quarterly or monthly examinations with excellent results, may be awarded medals and certificates by the Examination Yuan in addition to the scholarship. Article 15: These regulations shall be implemented on the date of promulgation by the Examination Commission and the Ministry of Education.

(Continuing Scholarship for Writings) A reporter from the Riri News Agency interviewed Wang Yongbin, Chairman of the Examination Commission, and Chen Daqi, Vice-Chairman, who stated that the first year's scholarship will be approximately 30,000 yuan, and funding has already been arranged. However, in the future, in addition to government allocations, it is hoped that all sectors will actively donate to avoid interruptions and to encourage participation. After the essay examination is successful, the second step will be to hold a scholarship for writings, which is of greater significance but more difficult to implement. This is because the level of various academic disciplines in China is generally inferior to that of the East and West, and it is not easy to recruit talents with the qualifications to evaluate writings domestically. In addition, the state has not paid much attention to academic awards in recent years, so it is difficult to arouse the interest of the academic community without good preparation. Currently, the three draft proposals for the Regulations for the National Construction Scholarship Committee, the Regulations for Essay Examinations, and the Regulations for the Fund Management Committee have all been submitted to the Central Political Council for review. Once they are passed, they can be formally prepared.

Fujian Education Director Protects Educational Talents 141

Only Changed the Principal of Xiamen Vocational High School

Since Zheng Zhenwen took office as the Director of the Fujian Provincial Department of Education, he has tried his best to protect educational talents. There have been no changes in the various bureaus and schools. Even in one or two schools, such as the Experimental Elementary School, the Agricultural and Forestry High School, and the Northern Fujian High School, where the principals resigned on their own, he still appointed the deans or directors of general affairs of each school to act as principals. It is said that after the school starts, he will personally go to his subordinates to inspect and then select talents to take over. However, the principal of Xiamen Vocational High School was recently changed. The reason for this is that the previous principal, Wang Shu, had poor performance since he took office. He received a monthly recurring expense of more than 2,000 yuan, but there were only more than 20 students in the entire school. The three classes offered, in addition to business, such as drawing and sewing, were mostly unnecessary. Chen Kezhong, an inspector from the Ministry of Education, and He Yunong, a military supervisor from the Provincial Department of Education, went to the school together for inspection last time and also believed that the performance was poor. The Provincial Department of Education has now appointed Wang Buai as the replacement. Wang graduated from a Japanese Higher Industrial School many years ago and has always had research on vocational education.

Local News

Ms. Luo Arrives in China 142

Examines Education and Visits Battlefields

丨Many Students Wishing to Study in England Contact Her丨

According to the Continental News, the China Committee of various universities in London recently sent Ms. Luo, a student, to China to promote friendship between the people of the two countries and to investigate certain educational issues. After arriving in Shanghai, she has been residing at her sister's residence at 2 Dofong Road for three weeks. In recent days, she has visited various educational institutions to examine everything and has also gone to libraries to engage in reference work. The lady once visited the ruins of the Oriental Library on Baoshan Road after it was burned down and was filled with sighs. In the past two weeks, Chinese students who want to study in England have often visited the lady, and many more have sent letters requesting assistance. They mistakenly believe that the lady is a representative of the China Committee of various universities and has the power to grant scholarships to Chinese students here. When they heard that the lady herself was also a student and that the only thing she could do for the students was to provide information on how to apply for this scholarship, according to the lady, the level of many of the students who visited was still insufficient. The lady also stated that Chinese women today are very eager to learn, but they are too modernized and things are trending towards extremes, which is not appropriate. When asked about the lady's opinions on companionate marriage and birth control, the lady replied that she was not concerned about such events. British women do not pay as much attention to this as their American sisters do. The lady plans to visit the Provincial First Normal School in Wuxi within a few days, and then plans to go to places such as Hangzhou and Nanjing to examine educational affairs. According to the lady, the China Committee of various universities plans to set up a Chinese student reception center in London for them to entertain friends and as a short-term residence. Everything will be done according to the YMCA method. According to the lady, she was born in Shanghai twenty-four years ago, and she feels particularly excited to revisit the old place.

Business School Specialized Freshmen Apply Enthusiastically 144

First Entrance Examination Yesterday

Must Continue to Test Next Monday and Tuesday

The National Shanghai Business School is enrolling students for the specialized course this time, and the number of applicants is very enthusiastic. Yesterday was the date of the examination, and more than 40 people came to take the exam in the rain. However, there are still many people who are unable to take the exam as scheduled due to the distance and being preoccupied with their jobs. They have requested an extension for the continued examination. Xu Peikun, the president of the school, has approved the request to avoid regrets for those who are eager to learn, and has scheduled the continued examination for next Monday and Tuesday (i.e., the 20th and 21st of this month) from 7:00 to 9:00 pm at Qingnian Middle School on Xiafei Road (opposite the Paris Grand Theatre). Therefore, those who are interested can still go to report for the examination. It is also heard that the most applicants this time are for the journalism specialty. In order to cultivate journalism talents, the school has hired lecturers who are experts in journalism. Various courses are striving for completeness, such as the latest Bingxun-style Chinese shorthand, which is also one of the selected courses. In terms of training, strictness is taken to cultivate noble journalists to meet the needs of the times.

Ministry of Education Rectifies Middle School Education Management 145

Strict Crackdown on Poor Examination Results

(Nanjing, 15th) The Ministry of Education issued a notice to the various provincial education departments, stating that the majority of middle school teaching in various places is following old routines, training and management are lax, academic results are not paid attention to during normal examinations, either teaching materials are used inappropriately, or teachers and textbooks are frequently changed, and there is no connection between the past and the future, resulting in low academic levels. The majority of students failed the recent joint examination. In addition to the grades of each school being revealed by the respective provincial education departments in accordance with the Regulations for the Joint Graduation Examination of Primary and Secondary School Students, the provincial education departments should quickly investigate the number of students taking the joint examination in each school. If more than half of them fail, the provincial education departments should give warnings to the respective schools depending on the circumstances, or order them to reorganize and improve teaching and management. If there is still no progress in the next joint examination results, all public and private middle schools should be strictly cracked down on or suspended separately. It is necessary to make the educational efficiency of each middle school gradually improve.

City Education Bureau Orders Schools to Use National Textbooks for Teaching Materials

Graduation Joint Examination This Semester Will Generally Use Chinese Questions 146

The City Education Bureau yesterday instructed the municipal and registered secondary schools in this city, saying, "It has been found that the textbooks used by various schools, except for foreign language courses that must use foreign language textbooks, should uniformly use national language textbooks for all other courses, and orders have been given in the past. However, according to recent investigations of the situation in various schools, the majority of those who abide by the Bureau's orders are the majority. Those who follow the old habits and use foreign language textbooks for non-foreign language courses still exist in some places. It is necessary to urgently reiterate the previous order. The textbooks for non-foreign language courses in the various schools should uniformly select national language textbooks from now on to facilitate teaching. Furthermore, the graduation joint examination to be held this semester will generally use Chinese questions, except for foreign language courses. The various schools should immediately guide students to prepare properly. It is necessary to order compliance with this order."

Physical Education Training Class 147

Instructor Fees Have Been Set

(Nanjing, 15th) The preparatory committee for the Ministry of Education's summer physical education training class held a meeting at the Ministry of Education at 5:00 pm on the 15th. The meeting was chaired by Chu Minyi, and the following matters were resolved: 1. The office of the committee will be temporarily set up in the Ministry of Education. It will be moved to the Department of Physical Education of National Central University one month before the meeting. 2. The curriculum and hiring of instructors were generally approved and will be finalized at the next meeting. 3. The method of recommending students: 4 from each province, 2 from each city, and the rest will be voluntarily recommended by the service organization. 4. The method of payment: tuition fee is 20 yuan, miscellaneous fee for electricity, tea, teaching materials and equipment is 10 yuan, personal equipment and clothing are self-provided. 5. All students will be boarded on campus. It is planned to hold another preparatory meeting next Wednesday at 5:00 pm.

Badminton Doubles Championship

Lin Qiu Was Eliminated Yesterday, Losing to the Portuguese 2-0 148

Seventeen to Eighteen丨Five to Fifteen

Lin Qiu Wins Exhibition Match

Carnevallo Willing to Teach Ball Skills

The Shanghai Badminton Championship began yesterday. In the first week of the doubles competition, Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai played against the two Portuguese, Xina and Xue Erfo. As a result of the fierce battle, Lin Qiu was unfortunately eliminated 2-0, 18-17, 15-5. Another game was played as an exhibition, and Lin Qiu won 15-5. Lin Baohua joined the singles competition. The first week was a bye, and the second week's competition will be held on the 25th.

(New Sport is Very Interesting) Badminton is a very popular sport among foreigners, but it is still a new sport among Chinese people. In order to promote it, the Badminton Club specially borrowed the court in Gezhi Public School on Beihai Road last night. Although it was drizzling, no less than three or four hundred people wanted to watch this new sport. The applause continued when they watched the tense and thrilling moments, indicating that they were very interested.

(The First Game Was a Pity to Lose) Xina and Xue Erfo had the right to serve first, and Clark was the referee. Xi Xue scored four points at once, and Lin Qiu regained three points. Then it became 5-4. In this tense situation, a situation of leaning left and right suddenly arose. Xi Xue suddenly broke out with 8-4. However, Qiu Feihai took turns serving and regained four points in a row, tying the score at 8-8. Unexpectedly, the opponent scored three points in a row again. At 12-10, the situation suddenly unfolded, and Lin Qiu chased to 12-12, and took the lead with 13-12. At this time, it was killed by the opponent. It was a pity, otherwise they would have won with two more points. Then it was 13-13, and Lin Qiu called a timeout. They were determined to win with five more points. Although Xi Xue had an advantage with 3-1, Lin Qiu killed the ball and added three points in a row, overtaking with 4-3. With one more point, they could also win. Unexpectedly, the opponent scored two points instead. In total, Lin Qiu lost the first game with 17-18, losing by only one point.

(The Second Game Was a Disaster) They were planning to fight hard to regain it in the second game, but unexpectedly, the situation changed drastically. Lin Qiu lost seven points in a row without paying attention. Although they regained two points at this time, Xi Xue went far away with 12-2. When it was Qiu Feihai's turn to serve, there was a great revival. He restored three points at once, but in the end, he lost again with 15-5, and was eliminated with 2-0.

(Lin Qiu Won the Exhibition Match) Finally, with the victory and defeat determined, the two sides played another game as an exhibition to entertain the audience. Lin Qiu went smoothly and got 9-2. The two Portuguese did not give in at all and fought hard, and it really became 9-9. As a result, Lin Qiu won 15-9, so the result can also be said to be 2-1.

(Qiu's Ball Skills Are Better Than Lin's) The two Portuguese have been playing for many years, so they are more mature in terms of connection and ball skills. The performance of Qiu and Lin is also quite good. The results of the first game show this. Qiu is even better than Lin. If Qiu joins the singles competition, the hope is greater than Lin. His kill ball is like his tennis ball, piercing the gaps and attacking people unprepared. The power of the kill ball is actually more interesting than tennis. Lin repeatedly tried to test the enemy with light pick in front of the net, but they were all broken by Xina. His smash is also not as stable as Qiu's. It is known that after this promotion, there will be great hope in the future. (Carnevallo's Talk) Tennis veteran Carnevallo told reporters that when he advocated badminton, there were only two teams established. Now it is popular and very interesting, which shows that there are people who love it. When Qiu was in Shanghai the year before last, Carnevallo joined Qiu in doubles and almost won the championship. Therefore, this year, he encouraged Qiu and Lin to participate to arouse the interest of the Chinese. Carnevallo is very willing to teach ball skills to the Chinese. If anyone wants to learn, please send a letter to the Shanghai Times Review Foreign Firm on Nanjing Road. Carnevallo can practice at the court. This is a great opportunity, so don't miss it.

Pan Yueying's Letter to Lu Lihua, Principal of Liangjiang School 151

Mr. Lihua,

I had the opportunity to meet you last time at the Zhejiang Construction Games. I was grateful that you did not abandon me and informed me of your plan to go to the United States this spring and invited Yueying to join you in the United States. I was entrusted with the training in your school. This is enough to show your enthusiasm for loving the country and loving talents. Yueying feels that her skills are insufficient to amaze people and her strength is insufficient to be competent. However, she is willing to do her best to contribute to the sports community in our country. In the end, because my mother was worried about me, I was unable to return to the east as instructed. I was idle at home and thought about what you asked Yueying to do, and I felt even more grateful and ashamed. So I asked about the preparations for going to the United States and also gave me a reply, instructing me to come to Shanghai as soon as possible to join the United States. At this time, Yueying decided to defy her mother's orders and come to Shanghai for the sake of the future of Chinese sports and for the kindness of your talent promotion. Since arriving at your school and revisiting all the facilities, I feel that there is too much lack of facilities that are essential for gymnasiums and physical education schools, and your school does not have them. The playground is no more than a few dozen feet, and the school building is precarious. To live with energetic sports people is truly a hero without a place to use his talents. Therefore, Yueying's feelings have changed again to your enthusiasm for running the school, your ambition to promote sports, and your love for talents. You do not focus on the school's own facilities, curriculum, and regulations. The improvement of the program and eagerly leading the small number of basketball talents in your school to expedition to the United States is to put vanity first and regard the school itself as unimportant. If this is the case, how can you achieve the popularization of sports and the success of the school? Yueying is deeply ashamed of you. If you do not allocate the funds raised for the trip to the United States to the construction of the school, dozens of students will benefit endlessly, and your success will be unlimited. Now, for the sake of sports in our country, for your success, for the future of your school, and for the students who have traveled thousands of miles to your school to study, I am sorry for not being able to respond to your expectations, and you can also take out Yueying's funds for going to the United States from the preparation fund and allocate it to the construction of your school as a small compensation. I am extremely frightened, ashamed and regretful, and I deeply pray for your understanding. I respectfully wish you a good day. 482 A special.

Member's Bowling Handicap Competition: Guo Renping Defeats All Competitors to Win the Championship 153

丨Mayor Wu Personally Donated a Large Silver Cup to Commemorate the Occasion丨

Wang Deming Worked Hard and Won the Second Place

丨Guo Won 160 to 120 in Last Night's Final丨

Shanghai Banking Club members enthusiastically participated in every member's bowling handicap competition, which was very popular. Thanks to the enthusiastic support of Mayor Wu, who donated a silver cup, the members' interest in the competition was even stronger than before. Large companies such as Xinxin and Daxin also donated silver cups and silver shields, and the names of the champions and runners-up were engraved to remain in the club forever to show immortality. Guo Renping and Wang Deming held the final last night at 6:00 pm, with Hu Yunlai as the referee. After an hour and fifteen minutes of competition, Guo reached his goal of 160 points first and won the championship. Mayor Wu's silver cup was also taken away by him. Wang took second place.

Victory Process 156

Mr. Guo won the championship, and his technique naturally had its merits and uniqueness. Compared to Mr. Wang, he was more experienced and steadier. His various shooting techniques were also quite proficient. However, luck is an indispensable indirect aid to victory and success, and Mr. Guo was particularly favored by it. Mr. Wang showed signs of improvement around the 53rd shot, but soon became silent again. In the end, both of them performed better in normal practice than in the finals, which is an unavoidable case of "stage fright." In the first 25 shots, Mr. Guo consistently had the upper hand, and Mr. Wang seemed to have lost his usual form. Mr. Guo was ahead with 57 to 25. In the next 25 shots, Mr. Guo continued to have great luck, while Mr. Wang still showed no improvement, with a difference of fifty or sixty points between them. In the final stage, Mr. Wang suddenly made an astonishing move, scoring 25 points in five shots, turning the situation around. The entire arena was stirred by this, but it was not sustainable. Mr. Guo remained focused and devoted himself to the target. Finally, he reached the goal of 160 points on the 78th shot. Looking back at Mr. Wang, he had also scored 120 points. Applause erupted, and the champion and runner-up shook hands and congratulated each other. The championship battle thus came to a close.

Shanghai Amateur Pistol Shooting Class C Competition 157

Chinese Li Gongrui Wins Championship

| Yesterday's final battle victory over Glaucl

Score: 500 to 381

The Shanghai Amateur Pistol Shooting Association's Class C Championship featured eighteen competitors, both Chinese and foreign. The final was held yesterday, starting at 5:30 PM, with Chinese competitor Li Gongrui against Glaucl. Mr. Li is the brother of Shanghai pistol king Li Gongying. He recently came to Shanghai from South China. His demeanor is similar to that of his younger brother, and his skills are also steady and commendable. He reached the Class C final on his first appearance in the Shanghai shooting scene, which is quite remarkable. In yesterday's final, he and Mr. Glaucl initially formed a parallel situation, with alternating leads. At the end of the first half, Mr. Glaucl had 250 points, and Mr. Li had 242 points. The competition resumed at 9:30 PM. Mr. Li rose magnificently, and with a pistol in hand, he was full of potential. He rarely missed a shot, moving forward from behind to take the lead. He eventually won by a large margin of 500 to 381 over Mr. Glaucl. The highest score for Mr. Glaucl was 42, and for Mr. Li, it was 26. Mr. Li's victory was due to his greater average score. It is said that among the Chinese who participated in this competition but were eliminated midway were Messrs. Qi, Zhu, and Xu.

Shanghai Basketball Association

Last Seven Minutes: Soochow Overcomes McTyeire 158

Soochow Almost Failed Last Night

36 to 33

Soochow vs. West China YMCA

Finals on Saturday

Last night's Class B Group 2 match between Soochow and McTyeire was crucial for determining the finals qualification. Soochow's performance was diminished due to unfavorable circumstances. Although they led 23 to 17 in the first half, Soochow only scored one point in the first thirteen minutes of the second half, while McTyeire scored fifteen, putting Soochow behind 24 to 22. The four to five hundred spectators were shocked and complained endlessly. After several hard battles, Soochow scored twelve consecutive points in the last seven minutes, finally winning 36 to 33. It was a close call! The cheers from the audience were even more enthusiastic.

(McTyeire frequently commits fouls) At the start, McTyeire frequently committed fouls, and Wu Guolin scored two consecutive baskets, giving Soochow an advantage. McTyeire actively resisted, showing no weakness. Kang, Deng, Mao, and Lei each displayed their talents, and Feng Nianhua and Sun Baoqing were not willing to fall behind, scoring three consecutive baskets, making the score 15 to 10, with Soochow leading by five points. At this time, Feng Nianhua suddenly suffered a foot injury and had difficulty walking, forcing him to leave the field. It can be said that fortunes are unpredictable and disasters are inconstant.

(Feng Nianhua leaves the field due to a foot injury) After Xiao Feng left the field, Lu Zhonghui and Lu Zhongen represented the forwards. From then on, they were evenly matched, each making contributions. The performance of both sides lacked brilliance. McTyeire lacked their usual courage, and Soochow also lacked their previous smooth style. Both were overly cautious, which made their movements unnatural. At the end of the first half, Soochow scored 23 points, and McTyeire scored 17 points.

(McTyeire's Major Player Ejected) As the second half began, Kang Deng first added a point for McTyeire.

Following that, Lu Zhongen of Soochow also returned a point. The back-and-forth battle saw little progress for either side. Wu Guolin of Soochow repeatedly shot, but all his shots missed the target. McTyeire's Mao Lei scored beautifully, and Kang Deng added another point, bringing the score to 23 to 24, with Soochow leading by only one point. But at this time, McTyeire's Bie Xupo was suddenly ejected for four fouls. With McTyeire losing this major player, everyone thought that Soochow could relax, but the reality was completely opposite to expectations.

(Soochow completely at a loss) After Bie Xupo left, he was replaced by Li Fu, and the game unexpectedly went smoothly. Kang Deng scored from afar, and the score suddenly exceeded Soochow's at 25 to 24. Mao Lei continued to contribute, making it 27 to 24. The foreign audience shouted wildly, very pleased. Seeing the unfavorable situation, Soochow called Feng Nianhua back in and replaced Lu Zhonghui, regaining their formation and trying to retaliate. But since Xiao Feng could not walk well, and the other players also seemed to be out of sorts, they attacked left and right, unable to get the ball into the basket, while McTyeire frequently broke through. Li Fu and Qin Bo scored successively, overwhelming Soochow with a large difference of 32 to 24.

(Seven Minutes to Reverse the Defeat) At this time, Soochow's bad luck had not ended. Lu Zhongen was also ejected for four fouls and was replaced by his younger brother, making the situation even more precarious, as if they were lost in a fog, not knowing what to do. Thirteen minutes had passed, with only seven minutes left. The audience was extremely anxious, stamping their feet and sighing. Soochow's players shook their heads and regretted. After several hard efforts and struggles, Feng Nianhua, with his injured foot, finally broke the deadlock. From then on, Soochow's spirit was greatly uplifted, and the cheers of support soared into the sky. The momentum then shifted, Sun Baoqing made two free throws, Wu Guolin scored three consecutive points, and Qian Jingyong and Feng Nianhua added five more points. The entire arena was filled with enthusiastic cheers and excitement. Until the bell rang to end the game, Soochow finally defeated McTyeire 36 to 33, winning the right to compete in the finals of the Class B Group 2 of the Shanghai Basketball Association.

(Soochow and West China YMCA to Face Off) After Soochow defeated McTyeire, they were crowned the champions of Class B Group 2. It is known that the winner of Class A Group 1 is the West China YMCA. The two teams will play a best-of-three series to compete for the "Besaipi Cup." The first game is scheduled for this Saturday (the 16th). It is hoped that Soochow will do its best to avenge its defeat against the West China YMCA in the association. The results of last night are as follows:

Guidelines for Submitting Articles to the National Products Weekly 160

(1) This publication solicits the following types of articles: (1) Investigations and research on national product factories and domestically produced raw materials; (2) Discussions on improving the production and sales of national products; (3) Records of lectures and talks on national products; (4) Introductions to new national product enterprises; (5) Interview records of national product businesses and their leaders; (6) National product news; (7) Other interesting and valuable articles, photos, and sketches related to national products.

(1) Submissions can be in any style, but emphasis should be placed on being concise and vivid. The length of each article should be around 500 characters, and at most, no more than 1,000 characters for those with special value.

(1) Submissions must be clearly written and use modern punctuation.

(1) Authors are free to choose whether to sign their names when submitting articles; however, they must indicate their real name and detailed address at the end of the article and affix their seal.

(1) The editor has the right to make deletions and revisions to submissions; those who do not wish to have their articles edited must state so in advance.

(1) Submissions will not be returned regardless of whether they are published; however, this does not apply to those who have stated in advance and have attached a self-addressed envelope with sufficient postage.

(1) A modest remuneration will be paid for published articles.

(1) Please send submissions directly to the Editorial Department of the National Products Weekly at Shen Bao.

Shen Bao National Products Weekly Issue 6 Published every Thursday

National Products Forum

The Domestic National Products Movement 162

— Pan Yang'an

……………………………………

The invasion of foreign goods and the filling of every household with imported goods is an undeniable fact. Even in some so-called modern families, whether it be clothing, food, housing, or transportation, all daily necessities cannot go a day without foreign goods. Setting aside the many serious problems of economic loss and excessive outflow, it is shameful that in our so-called independent country, there are many people who cannot survive without foreign goods, and many families who cannot live without foreign goods. This despicable habit and abnormal phenomenon are truly shameful!

Moreover, the families most severely controlled by foreign goods are mostly composed of intellectuals. Some say that the higher the level of education, the more effort is put into promoting foreign goods. The so-called advanced members of society are the first to fall into this situation, which is a great loss to society. At a time when the whole country is trying to save the country from disaster, especially in this year designated as the National Products Year, we should resolutely eliminate this bad habit first.

In terms of the consumption of national products, families have always occupied an important position. The national products industry must find its own way out, and naturally, efforts must be made in all aspects of production and sales. However, if every family can have the determination to use national products, it may be a way to increase revenue for the future of national products. Therefore, engaging in the domestic national products movement in this national products campaign is of great significance.

Regarding the implementation of the domestic national products movement, as long as everyone removes the inferiority of worshiping imported goods, using national products in life is not very difficult. Moreover, many emerging national products are substitutes, and sometimes they are cheaper and better than foreign goods. Just look at all the products of the recently opened China National Products Company. We have already found practical proof that is better than mere debate. Therefore, if we can understand this principle, and if the national product production industry can provide instructions on substitutes or the general use of national products, we will not have to make as much sacrifice as the Indians wearing felt blankets.

As for promotion, the success of one family's attempt is far more effective than countless flyers and slogans. In the first step, we certainly hope that intellectual women will lead by example because the word of mouth of the general public is better than you going door to door to promote! Expanding gradually from one family to relatives and friends, if such a good custom is established, its success will certainly not be limited to a short time! And we men! Do not abandon our responsibilities because we do not care about family matters. It is easier to persuade your wife or sisters than to persuade the general public. Since we are willing to make efforts in this national products campaign, we should naturally start with our own families.

Therefore, we must pay attention to the domestic national products movement; in every family, establish the morality and belief of "I love national products, I buy national products, I use national products!"

Investigation

The Recent Situation of the Sino-Japanese Cotton Industry 163

— Yin Ge

Recently, due to various factors such as war and floods, the Chinese cotton industry has been greatly affected, while the Japanese cotton industry in Shanghai has been even more depressed. Before the outbreak of the Shanghai war, Japanese merchants had 56,000 pieces in stock. Production was suspended for three months after the outbreak of the war. After resuming operations in April, sales were very limited due to strong resistance to Japanese goods in our country. Moreover, the independence of the puppet state's customs duties also had an impact on Japanese cotton yarn in Shanghai. In the past, resistance to Japanese goods could not last long because Chinese cotton yarn could only meet half of the demand. After about half a year, Japanese goods would definitely be sold well again. This time, however, it is different. The Dong'an incident was not resolved, and the Shanghai incident followed. The anti-Japanese movement is more profound. In addition, the Yangtze River flood and the development of national products are all sufficient to hinder the sales of Japanese cotton yarn. Therefore, the Japanese cotton industry in Shanghai is almost in a state of collapse. The cotton yarn produced by Chinese merchants has increased by 34,800 pieces per month, and the inventory has increased to more than 80,000 pieces, which is different from the Japanese factories' remaining 30,000 pieces. However, Japanese cotton yarn factories are well-managed, and their companies that operate the cotton industry have sales networks all over the world, making it easy to develop new markets. On the other hand, Chinese factories have less capital and fewer public reserves, and they often cannot proceed smoothly. It is hoped that they will help each other and study technology carefully to compete with the Japanese. Do not allow the enemy to invade due to negligence in the last five minutes. This will greatly benefit the future of the national economy.

Let Me Introduce a Few Kinds of Homespun Cloth 164

— Chen Jingyu

Clothes are nothing more than tools to protect the body. As long as they are worn to cover the limbs and keep the body warm, they can be passable. Why must we use expensive materials and spend a lot of money! Then, if we want economical and durable fabrics, we should look to the homespun cloth produced in the countryside!

Speaking of homespun cloth, it originally belongs to the products of our Songjiang area. There are many different kinds and patterns! When the exhibition was held in Shanghai last year, the displayed homespun cloth reached more than one hundred and several tens of types, most of which were produced in our Songjiang area. And the counties of "Fengxian," "Nanhui," and "Chuansha" in Pudong are especially famous for producing homespun cloth! Taking our "Fengxian" as an example, the clothes that the villagers wear daily, which can be seen, have at least thirty or fifty kinds of colors and patterns. Recently, there are even some women with intelligent nature who have actually come up with new ideas and made inventions. They have slightly improved the existing looms and added foot pedals. (Originally two, now increased to four). From this, we can see that the yarn is increased, and the weaving is complicated; and the results produced are becoming more and more excellent! Now there are several new products that were not seen in last year's exhibition; and their ingenuity and pleasing appearance actually surpass foreign goods! I am here to introduce them to you, for the purchase of the national product company.

Water Wave Cloth: Its pattern is curved like waves in the water. To put it bluntly, it looks like a herringbone serge. It is woven with double-layer fine yarn, and its texture is thick and soft. It is best to make inner clothing! But it is also very elegant to dye it into colors and make long robes for men and women. At first glance, it is almost like serge, but it lacks luster.

Chicken Feather Towel: The color yarn is interspersed with white yarn to weave the shape of chicken feathers. It is quite beautiful for women to use as cheongsam! It is also very suitable for young men's jackets and children's clothing!

Eye Cloth: It is also made of colored yarn and white yarn, and the whole fabric is patterned as if it is full of human eyes. Clothes made of it are suitable for women and children!

Although I am not a member of the "Cloth Clothing Association," I am one of those who advocate cloth clothing. Since there is such a good homespun cloth at present, all of us Chinese people should unite and strive for frugality at this time of economic decline and repeated foreign insults! Engage in vegetarianism and cloth clothing. If there is a need, we should go to the national product company to purchase it, and donate the money saved as much as possible to the anti-Japanese volunteer army in the Northeast, so as to increase their courage to fight! And to relieve the national crisis!

National Products Talk

Returning from the China National Products Company 165

— Zhou Chengxun

Every time I walk on Nanjing Road, which is dazzlingly lit by neon lights, I always see signs full of "European and American Goods" and "Western Products," which suffocate people. Since the China National Products Company was established a week ago, it has forcibly attracted batches of fellow countrymen who are fascinated by European and American styles, and they have deeply engraved the idea of "I love national products" in their minds. In this year of national crisis and flooding of imported goods, this is indeed a gratifying thing.

The history of Chinese people shouting "Promote national products" has been around for a long time, but there have been very few who have organized, principled, and down-to-earth to do something. The China National Products Company has united many well-known national product factories, gathered many talented people who are determined to save the country, and cooperated to do it near the three towering cannons, regardless of success or failure. Let's not expect it to have a huge effect, but at least it has given our compatriots a shot in the arm.

On the day the China National Products Company opened, I went to visit it. Judging from the fact that the customers or guests were so crowded that it was impossible to move, and the staff were so busy that they didn't even have time to eat, this unprecedented grand occasion was truly the supreme harvest of the national product industry. But whether it was the power of the words "Opening Discount of 10%" or indeed the stimulation of our compatriots' patriotism is a question? We should spend some effort to answer it.

Past facts tell us that the effect of all national product exhibitions cannot satisfy us very much. This is all caused by the organizers having profit-seeking ideas and our compatriots holding curious thoughts. To answer the above question, it all depends on the efforts of the company's executives and the sincere understanding of our compatriots.

We sincerely wish the China National Products Company can recover the declining national product industry and spread the seeds of saving the country in the minds of our compatriots!
